A Pair of Lovers

A Man with a Wife Wishes to be a Partner in Death, But Fails 125

Twice Attempted Suicide in a Hotel, Both Times Surviving

Drafted Elegiac Couplets that Provoke a Chuckle

Fu Meizhen, a woman from Ningbo, is 29 years old, with delicate features. Her home is located at an unmarked address in Chenjiadu, Zhoujiaqiao, West Shanghai. She graduated from Chendu Elementary School there. Recently, due to abuse by her stepmother, she was betrothed to a man surnamed Zhu. In September of this year, she fell in love with Shi Shoudao, a 23-year-old clerk from Chongming at the nearby Yucheng Sauce Garden. They fell in love at first sight, and Shi lured her to a room in the Asia Hotel on Hankou Road. They had a physical relationship once and then made a vow of eternal love. However, Shi was already married and his parents were very strict. Later, the owner of Yucheng Garden found out and fired him. Shi and Fu Meizhen could not achieve their goal of getting married. Later, he opened a room alone in the Asia Hotel and attempted suicide by poison, but was rescued by his elder brother and taken home. However, he could not sever his love with Miss Fu, and they often exchanged letters or met to talk on the road. However, Miss Fu already had a fiancé, and Shi also had a wife at home. After discussing it between themselves, they sighed and cried, unable to think of a solution. On the tenth of this month, Shi Shoudao bought one and a half yuan of American opium in a village and secretly agreed to meet Miss Fu at Room 23 of the Kunming Hotel at No. 35 Kunming Road. Shi explained his feelings to Fu Meizhen and wrote several suicide notes. In his suicide note, Shi Shoudao stated the reasons for his suicide: 1. I committed bigamy. 2. I am obstructed by my parents. 3. I wish to be buried with Fu Meizhen after death. He also wrote two elegiac couplets: 1. "Two hearts were willing but could not be together, Huai'an (i.e., Miss Meizhen) is famous as a dazzling pearl, Farewell, my affectionate younger sister." 2. "Dying together and being buried together is a grand reunion, Life is a dream, respectfully by Shi Shoudao, an unrighteous person." After these two couplets were completed, one was placed on each coffin. Then, they divided the raw opium in half and ate it before going to sleep. Unexpectedly, they vomited almost everything out after a while. They thought they could not commit suicide in Room 23, so they changed to Room 28 the next morning. Shi went to the village again to buy three more pieces of opium Yuan and brought them back to the hotel. That night, the two continued to take the drug and slept in the same bed, waiting for death. At around 11:00 AM early the next morning (i.e., the 12th), Song Baofang, a tea waiter at the hotel, knocked on the door, intending to clean the room, but there was no response. Realizing something was wrong, he used a kitchen knife to pry open the door. He was shocked to see them lying stiff on the bed. Miss Fu was lying face down, her complexion already gray. Shi Shoudao had a trouser belt tied around his neck, his eyes closed and silent. Song first untied the belt, pushed him, but he did not speak, but his body was still warm. He then reported to the front desk and telegraphed Huishan Patrol Room, which sent Chinese detective Xu Shutian and Western detective to rush to the scene. Shi Shoudao was taken to Tongren Hospital, and the woman, Fu Meizhen, was taken to Shanghai Convalescent Hospital on Old Baffle Road for treatment. Fortunately, it was not too late, and emetic medicine was used to vomit out the opium juice. They gradually recovered the day before yesterday, and Shi Shoudao was taken into custody in the patrol room. Fu Meizhen was taken back by her father, Fu Quanyou. Yesterday morning, the patrol room sent Shi Shoudao to the Third Criminal Court of the First Special District Court. Zhang Tianyin, the patrol room lawyer, stated the previous situation and claimed that the patrol room had filed public charges on the two counts of seduction and instigation of suicide. He presented the confiscated suicide note, elegiac couplets, trouser belts, etc. for investigation. Then, Song Baofang, the tea waiter at Kunming Hotel, testified about what had happened. Fu Quanyou also testified that he had four sons and three daughters with his previous wife, and Meizhen was the youngest. His current wife, Yin, had been married for ten years and also had a daughter. Meizhen was indeed betrothed to a man surnamed Zhu. He did not know about her relationship with the defendant. In September, the daughter did not return home for one night, claiming to have stayed at her sister's place, so he did not ask in detail. A few days ago, the daughter went shopping and did not return. Later, he saw it reported in the newspaper and knew about it. He went to the hospital to pick up his daughter, etc. The woman, Fu Meizhen, wearing a patriotic cloth cheongsam and civilized satin shoes, hung her head and said that the defendant had asked her to go to the hotel to commit suicide, so she had to obey. Shi Shoudao confessed that he committed suicide with the woman because he had no face to see his parents, so he took this action. He asked for consideration. After Judge Shen Bingrong gave a sincere warning to both parties, he ordered them to start the debate and then ordered them to be remanded in custody and a date set for sentencing. He also ordered Fu Quanyou to take his daughter back and advise her, and not to beat her.

Clerk Sees a Large Sum of Money and Gets Evil Intentions, Embezzles Funds and Falsely Reports Being Kidnapped 126

Covered Hands and Feet with Mud

Lies Thrown into the River

Accomplice Has Also Been Arrested

But the Stolen Money Is Still Missing

At around 12:00 AM on Saturday night, a man from Jiangbei, Lü Wenbiao, reported to the Xinza Patrol Room that he was passing by the entrance of Siwenli on Xinza Road when he was suddenly encountered by two kidnappers who threatened him with guns, dragged him onto a car, covered his head with a coat, and drove quickly into the countryside. They robbed him of more than 1,000 yuan in cash and silver he was carrying, tied his feet with rope, and threw him into a river. Later, he untied the ropes himself and came to the patrol room to report, etc. Western Detective Chief Bao Tai, Chinese Detective Zhao Fuhai, and Detective Bao Derong found Lü's words suspicious, and there was only a little mud on one hand and one foot. They took Lü to investigate in the Siwenli area, and there was no kidnapping. Under strict questioning, he finally confessed to embezzling public funds and falsely reporting a robbery. According to Lü, he was 27 years old and lived at No. 62 Taiyang Temple, Zhabei. He was a clerk at the Japanese-owned Harada Shanghai Branch at No. 362 Zhafu Road, earning a monthly salary of 18 yuan. At 11:30 AM on the 14th of this month, a Japanese man named Harada gave Lü a check for 1,353 taels, 3 mace, and 7 fen from the Yokohama Specie Bank in Shanghai, instructing him to deliver goods at Siwenli, Datong Road. He met a friend named Xu Zirong on the way and had an evil idea. Lü's monthly salary was not enough to cover his expenses, and now that he had a large sum of money on him, he might as well embezzle it privately and spend it, and then find a way to report the robbery to the patrol room, so that the shopkeeper could be deceived. Lü was blinded by greed and acted recklessly. Lü and Xu went to the Yokohama Specie Bank in Shanghai. Xu waited outside the door, and Lü went inside and received a silver note for 500 taels, and the rest was in cash. He walked out of the bank and handed all the money to Xu Zirong, agreeing to meet at the Santai Inn on Jiujiang Road in the evening to divide the money, and then they dispersed. Lü went home, rode a bicycle to the side of Xiaohang behind the Yong'an Yarn Factory on Changping Road in West Shanghai, tied his feet with rope, walked towards the riverbank, and then smeared mud on his hands and feet, and then untied the rope and reported to the patrol room, etc. The Chinese and Western detectives arrested Xu Zirong, but Xu denied it. Lü and Xu were both taken into custody and sent to the Simple Court of the First Special District Court yesterday morning. Qian Xunjiu, the lawyer for the patrol room, detailed the above situation and stated that the stolen money was still missing, so he requested permission to postpone the investigation. Bao Tai, the western detective, then complained about the investigation. Judge Zhan Liangce examined the confession and ordered Lü and Xu to be detained and interrogated again in seven days after the investigation was completed.

Murderer Executed by Hanging 127

Zhang Zimei Recalls His Wife and Children Before Death

Sends a Letter Asking His Uncle to Take Care of Them

Jiang Haitao, who was previously employed as a driver at the First Special District Court, lived at No. 130 Shanjia Garden, Guling Road. At 8:30 AM on September 15 of last year, Jiang went from his home to the court to handle business. Before he had walked a few steps, he was suddenly stabbed several times by his enemy, Zhang Zimei, with a sharp knife. Because the injuries were to vital points, he died on the spot. The murderer was caught on the spot, sent to the First Special Court for interrogation, and the facts were clear. Zhang Zimei was sentenced to death and reported to the Jiangsu Provincial Government for approval. Yesterday afternoon, the date for execution had arrived. The Xinza Patrol Room sent detectives to escort Zhang to the Third Criminal Court of the Special Court. Judge Shen Shanzeng ascended the seat and announced to Zhang that he had been ordered to carry out the death penalty today. He asked him if he had any last words for his family. Zhang said that he was 31 years old, from Tongzhou, and had previously worked as a driver. He lived on Kangnaidao Road, had a wife and two children, and asked if his uncle could be brought in for a face-to-face conversation. As there was not enough time, the court wrote a letter on his behalf, notifying Zhang Aliang, a driver at the Gordon Road Patrol Room (i.e., his uncle), asking him to take care of his wife and children, and he had nothing else to say. Judge Shen ordered him to be sent to the Local Court for execution. The Chinese and Western detectives then took Zhang down, along with the case file and photos, and escorted him by car directly to the Caohiejing execution ground. The Procuratorate of the Local Court was also notified to send a prosecutor to supervise the execution of the law enforcement police on the spot. After re-examining Zhang, he was ordered to be executed. Because Zhang was convicted of murder, he was to be hanged as an example, and the body exposed overnight, and a coffin prepared the next day for burial.

A corresponding letter is replied for you to take note.

Inland Waterways to Suzhou, Wuxi, Changzhou, and Dangkou Have Been Blocked by Ice for Four Days 129

Most Ice Obstructions are Near Gaodian

Various Shipping Companies Have Sent Ships to Break the Ice

Since the 13th of this month, the weather in Shanghai has been severely cold. The cold and ice in the Suzhou and Changzhou area is even worse, and there is also more snow. The reporter happened to go to Suzhou on that day. From the 14th, the small steamers on the Suzhou-Shanghai, Shanghai-Wuxi, Dangkou routes, as well as the Shanghai-Changzhou-Yixing-Jiangyin routes, were completely blocked by ice and could not operate. The inland water transportation from Shanghai to Suzhou, Wuxi, Changshu, Dangkou, etc., has been completely cut off by ice. On the 14th, the reporter planned to go to Wuxi from Suzhou, but because all inland waterway民船 and航轮 were completely suspended, there was no way to return to his hometown. More than a hundred ships and passenger craft were frozen mid-journey, and as a result, it was difficult for them to advance or retreat. Since the 14th, ships carrying rice, livestock, vegetables, etc., from various towns have been cut off from Suzhou and Shanghai. Fortunately, the small steamers on the Zhejiang routes to Shanghai are still open, so there are still a few rice boats reaching Shanghai. Yesterday, the reporter went to various inland waterway Shipping Companies to inquire. It was said that the Shanghai-Suzhou, Shanghai-Wuxi, Shanghai-Changshu, and Dangkou boats were still blocked by ice and could not pass. Among the blocked inland waterways, the most ice obstructions were near Gaodian. It has been four days and there is still no hope of thawing and通行. Currently, the various shipping companies have sent a large number of ships to the ice-obstructed area to break the ice, intending to use this gradually warming weather to open航道. They are also planning to transship a large number of stranded passengers. Also, fearing that the journey will not be peaceful at the end of the year, and that there will be unexpected dangers to the stranded ships, the Jiangsu Inland Water Police have been asked to send ships to protect them.

The Case of Robbery of a Large Amount of Cotton in the Suzhou Creek at Van Royal Ferry is Solved 131

Recovered the Original Cotton

The Fence Also Arrested

Mitsui & Co., a Japanese firm, hired a large barge belonging to boat owner Ding Guantong on the 12th of this month. They loaded 110 bales of cotton, valued at 15,600 gold dollars, from the Hongsheng Warehouse in Pudong. The barge sailed to the Suzhou Creek in front of the Toyota Spinning Mill at the east end of Zhongshan Road in the West of Shanghai and moored there. They planned to unload the cotton at the Toyota Spinning Mill the next day. However, due to heavy snow and ice, unloading was difficult, and it was decided to deliver the cotton on the 14th. Unexpectedly, at 1:10 AM on the 13th, more than a dozen robbers suddenly appeared, tied up the boat owner and crew, and locked them in the rear cabin. They also dragged the escorting petition policeman, Li Xiaolian, ashore. Then, they sailed the boat to a location near the barracks. Seventy-two bales of cotton were robbed, loaded onto a truck, and the robbers fled. Afterwards, the boat owner reported the robbery to the Sixth District Public Security Bureau and requested the arrest of the thieves and the recovery of the stolen goods. This was previously reported. Recently, detectives from the City Public Security Bureau discovered that the robbers were hiding in Room 22 of the Chunjiang Hotel in the vegetable market street of the French Concession. The detectives rushed to the French Concession Police Department to request assistance in the arrest. Inspector Jin Jiulin, along with detective Zhang Ziqiao and others, went to the Chunjiang Hotel and arrested a robber named Wu Desheng. Wu confessed that he had sold all the stolen goods to Sun Hongcai, a resident of Haimen Road in Weier Meng Road. The detectives then arrested Sun and the doorman, Gong Yilin, and recovered the original 72 bales of stolen cotton, bringing them to the police station. Yesterday morning, they were escorted to the First Criminal Court of the Second Special Court. First, Yuan Jiahan, a lawyer from the police station, presented the case, stating that the defendants Sun Hongcai and Gong Yilin had committed the crime of receiving stolen goods under Article 376 of the Criminal Law and requested an investigation. Then, a detective from the Public Security Bureau described the circumstances of the robbery and requested permission to transfer the defendants to their custody for interrogation. During the interrogation, Sun Hongcai confessed that Wu Desheng had transported the cotton to his residence as collateral for 3,000 yuan, and he was unaware that it was stolen. Gong Yilin confessed that he was just a doorman and did not dare to help receive stolen goods. Wu Desheng confessed that boat owner Ding Guantong had entrusted him to sell the cotton on his behalf and that he had sold it to Sun Hongcai for 3,000 yuan. Judge Xiong verified the confessions and asked the police station lawyer for his opinion on the Public Security Bureau's request to transfer the defendants. Lawyer Yuan replied that the police station would not object if the Public Security Bureau sent an official document to request the transfer. At this point, the court ordered the defendants to be returned to custody and scheduled another hearing for the 19th. The court also ordered the Public Security Bureau to submit an official document to the court for review.

Minutes of the Standing Committee Meeting of the Jiangsu Rice Association 132

The Joint Association of Rice Merchants of Jiangsu, Nanjing, and Shanghai held its 15th Standing Committee Meeting of the second session yesterday at 2:00 PM in Cuixiu Hall. The committee members present were Zhu Zixiang, Zhao Zixin, Lu Zhuqing, Qian Jingsheng, Zhu Zhaoqi, Gong Zhaoming, Fu Qiangeng, Yan Xiaoquan, Lu Gongquan, (Zhu Zixiang substituting), Pang Bosen (Yan Xiaoquan substituting), Li Zhongchen (Zhao Zixin substituting), Zhang Nianxuan (Gong Zhaoming substituting), Cai Yukun, and thirteen others. Zhao Zixin chaired the meeting, and the usual procedures were followed. Committee member Zhu Zixiang proposed that the Shanghai Rice Merchants Association would implement a new system of measurement starting February 1st, with the original Haihu reduced by 15%. The same standard should be applied to merchants in the inland to avoid disputes. The chairman then stated that the Xidi measurement was almost the same as the new Shanghai standard, and a slight modification of the old measurement could be applied, which would save a lot of money. However, only a few merchants from the inland, such as Wuxi, were present today, and a circular should be sent to all members to make slight changes according to the new Shanghai standard to ensure consistency. The proposal was approved and passed. Then, Committee member Zhu reported on the 21st year's income and expenditure accounts and future methods of increasing revenue and reducing expenditure. The committee members felt that with the closure of the meeting approaching, the tasks were too numerous and complicated to be resolved hastily, and the matter should be discussed again at the next Standing Committee meeting.

The Police Department Seeks Arrest

The following two Chinese men are wanted by the Public Concession Police Department for the crime of fraud and obtaining money. These two men impersonate tax bureau inspectors and visit shops, requesting to see the account books. At the same time, they show a circular badge with the Kuomintang star emblem to impersonate real inspectors. When they find that the books do not have the appropriate stamps, the first of the two men tries to solicit fines from the shop owner. (A) is about 28 years old, about 5 feet 5 inches tall, with a slender build and black hair parted in the middle. He was last seen wearing a black serge suit, white collar, black tie, and black leather shoes, and he speaks with a Cantonese accent. (B) is about 27 years old, about 5 feet 3 inches tall, with a small build. He was last seen wearing a light brown silk robe, a gray Russian hat, and black Chinese shoes, and he speaks with a Cantonese accent.

Sudden Snowfall Yesterday in This Port 134

It had been snowing in this port for several days, ceasing only the day before yesterday (the 15th), but then it turned overcast again and the cold wind did not abate. Yesterday morning, starting at 7:00 AM, it suddenly began to snow again, with great force. The sound of snow falling on the roof tiles could be heard clearly, and the snow felt slightly painful as it landed. The snow stopped at 11:00 AM, but then it turned into rain, drizzling throughout the day and not stopping until night.

China Electric Company Refuses to Sign for Workers' Tonics and Medicines 135

According to past practice, if employees of the China Electric Company became ill due to their work and needed to take leave for medical treatment, the company would provide preferential treatment, stipulating that the company would be responsible for medical expenses. However, the expense claims had to be signed by General Manager Lu of the company before a worker could obtain the medicine from the pharmacy. Yesterday afternoon, at about 1:00 PM, Chen Sanyi, the foreman of the company's cold-working shop, had a prescription with medicine expenses totaling about 20 yuan. He went to General Manager Lu for signature, but after reviewing the prescription, General Manager Lu refused to sign because the prescription was for tonics and supplements. Unexpectedly, the foreman Chen Sanyi became enraged in the general manager's office, smashing the glass window. At that time, a certain member of the labor union and the police team stationed at the company tried to persuade him, but Chen still refused to comply. Subsequently, the company notified the Second District by telephone, and District Chief Jin, along with Officer Fan and a police officer, rushed to the company and took the foreman Chen Sanyi to the district for interrogation.

The Verdict in the Embezzlement Case Against Managers and Others of the Riyue Bank 136

After the founder Huang Chujiu passed away, the Shanghai Riyue Bank and the Gongfa Company both went bankrupt. Creditors filed lawsuits in the Civil Court of the former French Concession Court, requesting to recover their deposits. The court appointed accountants Pan Zhaobang and Wu to liquidate all the accounts of the bank and the company. It was discovered that the account books of the Riyue Bank had been tampered with by the manager Chen Zhiquan, the accountant Chen Yuqing, Chen Xunqing, and Huang Xianzhong through collusion and embezzlement of funds. The accountants then filed a criminal lawsuit with the court, accusing Chen and the other three. The trial was not concluded, and the Second Special District Court was established to take over the case files and continue the trial. Because the lawsuit was initiated by the accountants, it did not comply with the litigation procedure. The creditors then legally initiated a private prosecution, accusing Chen and the other three of forging documents, embezzlement, and other crimes. After the trial concluded, the defendants were found not guilty because their actions had not affected the creditors' rights. The plaintiffs, the creditors, were dissatisfied with the verdict and, through their lawyers Xu Yannian and others, filed an appeal with the Third Branch of the Jiangsu High Court. The High Court, based on the appeal, summoned the original case files and first summoned the defendants to open an investigation court. After the interrogation was completed, the court summoned both parties yesterday afternoon. Presiding Judge Zhou, along with judges Guo and Zhu, and the prosecutor, convened a collegiate court for trial. Qin Zemin, a lawyer representing the creditor group, stated the intent of the prosecution. Then, lawyers Xu Yannian, Yan Luqing, Dong Chi, and others spoke successively, stating the circumstances of the case. The officials then interrogated the defendants Chen Zhiquan and others and also summoned accountant Pan to be questioned about the discovery of the tampering of the account books and the embezzlement. The court then ordered the debate to begin. After the lawyers for the plaintiffs debated, the defendants were defended by lawyer Tan Yigong. The court then declared the debate concluded and awaited a scheduled verdict.

Robbery and Assault in Jiangwan Town 137

| Wang Xingsheng's Life is in Danger |

In a bungalow on Zhujiang Street in Jiangwan Town, the home of local resident Qiu Yonglin was suddenly invaded by five robbers at around 4:30 AM yesterday morning. One robber held a handgun and stood guard outside the door, while the other robbers rushed into the house, dragging the residents, both men and women, old and young, out of their beds, arbitrarily threatening them, and looting freely. After the looting, they broke into the inner room of Hailin, Yonglin's younger brother, in the outer wing. At that time, Yonglin was slightly away from the robbers and shouted for help loudly. His neighbor, Wang Xingsheng, 58 years old, suddenly heard the shouting and opened the door to peek outside. He was spotted by the robber standing guard outside the door, who immediately fired a shot, hitting Wang in the chest. The bullet pierced his back, and blood gushed out like a spring. He collapsed on the spot. After the robbery, the robbers fled with their loot in a southeast direction. It is reported that the Qiu family suffered significant losses, but the exact amount is unknown. The injured man was sent to the Tongren Hospital for treatment by car yesterday afternoon. It is said that Wang lost too much blood and, being nearly sixty years old, his injuries are critical.

Land Agent Sentenced for Fraudulently Collecting Grain Tax 138

Ming Meili, an elderly American woman residing at No. 464 Lafayette Road in the French Concession, purchased six mu, six fen, six li, and zero hao of land in the 13th tu of the 25th bao in South Shanghai. The land agent, Cai Lingen, who had since been removed from his post of land agent in the said tu, had been responsible for collecting the grain tax on this land. But it was discovered that during the previous year, Cai had privately created fake grain tax receipts, defrauding the woman of 349.8 yuan in grain tax. In August of the same year, Cai sent the American woman a letter in English, falsely stating that the government was experiencing economic difficulties due to the Shanghai War and was pre-collecting next year's grain tax, totaling 199.89 yuan. The matter was reported, yesterday morning, Judge Xiong presided over the court and sentenced Cai Lingen to eight months in prison for the crime of continuous use of forged official documents. The number of days of detention prior to the final judgment will be used to offset the sentence, with two days of detention equaling one day of imprisonment.

Reader's Advisor

How to Maintain Public Order? 139

| Letter from Mr. Hu Liangcun |

In our Yi County, bandits have been rampant in recent years, and robberies are frequently heard. The people cannot defend themselves, and the government cannot solve the cases, resulting in an increase in banditry and widespread public unease. The root cause of the disaster lies in the fact that our community’s poor social structures lead to the people's bad financial behaviors; spending a fortune to build a house and one hundred taels of silver to buy land. Such extravagance tempts bandits to get involved. As for the local armed forces, although there is a county government police force to maintain order, in reality, it is not only equivalent to zero, but also causes us endless sighs. Last year, a portion of the police force mutinied, and after the mutiny, they were reorganized. What will the social order rely on? At this time, what methods should be used to defend ourselves? I respectfully ask you for guidance!

Reply: The problem of "people's self-defense" has two meanings: one is to defend oneself against bad politics and the exploitation of landlords and gentry; the other is to defend oneself against bandits. The letter is intended to defend oneself against "bandits." In fact, we must understand the causes of bandits before we can discuss the way to defend ourselves. The reason why bandits are so numerous is because: ㈠ China's rural areas have been directly and indirectly exploited by the commodity economy of capitalist imperialism. The rural areas are bankrupt day by day. For example, this year there has been a bumper harvest everywhere, but the government has borrowed a large batch of American wheat. The price of wheat in the market has suffered a sharp drop, and although farmers have harvested a lot of grain, they are still living through a famine year. Farmers cannot even sell their land. ㈡ The harsh taxes are increasing day by day. Farmers have to take out at least 50% of their annual grain harvest to pay taxes. ㈢ The exploitation of landlords and the exploitation of usury make it even more impossible for tenant farmers to survive, and ㈣ now poppies are being forced into collection everywhere. It is said that the opium tax collected in various parts of Huizhou amounts to eight or nine million a year. With such layers of exploitation, how can rural areas not go bankrupt quickly? In addition, imperialists oppress the people layer by layer and collude with Chinese warlords. They are doing evil there every day. Today there is a civil war here, and tomorrow Japanese soldiers are fighting there. The national economy is completely in a state of decline, which will naturally affect the rural areas. As a result, the decline of rural areas is becoming increasingly apparent. Furthermore, in a good way, the means of capitalist production have been widely adopted along the Yangtze River, using steam plows, mechanical irrigation, and electricity. As a result, the unemployment of laborers in rural areas is increasing day by day. A small portion has gone to the cities, and a large portion are still wandering in the villages. They are unwilling to "sit and wait for death," and there are two paths ahead: one is to join the army, and the other is to become bandits. This is a common phenomenon in China, and the situation in your area is probably the same. Therefore, unemployed farmers can wear military uniforms and become county police officers, or take off their military uniforms and become bandits. Zheng Banqiao said it well, "Bandits are also poor people!" Today, to defend ourselves against bandits, we must think of the entire rural economy of China and the entire economic and political situation of China. The following are some short-term measures: ㈠ Demand that the government eradicate harsh taxes and miscellaneous levies; ㈡ Oppose any opium seedling taxes, and the responsibility for banning opium should be borne jointly by local civilian groups, so as to ensure that the rural economy is not destroyed by opium planting; ㈢ Strictly oppose the usury and inhuman exploitation of landlords and commercial capital: ㈣ All public land in the area should be managed jointly by public groups and distributed to unemployed farmers for cultivation. The ownership should belong to the area, and the farmers should only pay 10% of the land rent to the area as funds for public services; ㈤ The county police should be completely disbanded and taught to cultivate public land. As for the responsibility for local security, it should be organized jointly by the local people to form a local security team, with each household contributing manpower. However, the power must be held by the people and not be controlled by local tyrants and evil gentry. Otherwise, it will become a disguised form of the county police team. If so, on the one hand, an economic source will be opened up for the rural areas, and on the other hand, unnecessary suffering will be eliminated. The rural economy can be maintained to a considerable extent, unemployment will be reduced, and there may also be fewer bandits. However, this is still a "treating the head when it hurts" approach. If you want to fundamentally "defend yourself," then you must fundamentally reform the current system. We will have the opportunity to talk about it again.

How to Deal With Debt Collectors? 140

| Letter from Mr. Peng Zemin |

I have a mother, an older sister, and a younger brother. My father died when I was four years old, and we have been living with my mother in hardship ever since. In the past, our lives, my sister's marriage, and my and my brother's schooling all depended on the inheritance of twenty-four mu of thin land. The harvest from the twenty-four mu of land is estimated to be about eighty yuan per year. The repair of the oil mill on the land and the living expenses of a family of four all depend on this annual income of eighty yuan. In these twenty years, natural and man-made disasters have constantly affected our remote inland area. The economic aggression of imperialism has affected the domestic rural economy. With an annual income of eighty yuan, no matter how frugal we are, it is not enough to support our lives! It is a pity that my mother led us, a group of young people, and had to struggle hard! At first, we asked friends and relatives to join hui (according to the local people's economic mutual assistance method, such as asking for a hui of one hundred yuan, ten friends must be invited, and it is held once every ten months, the leader of the hui has the right to get the first hui without giving hui interest) to maintain the temporary situation, but when it came time to run the hui, we could not come up with this large amount of money to make up the hui, so we had to pawn the land and engage in interest loans (interest of three points) to make up for it. In this way, we made up for the symptoms but did not cure the disease and struggled through more than ten years. Now, although I have a job, my annual income is only fifty yuan. My family has a total debt of more than three thousand seven hundred yuan. Even if we sell the land and the house at an estimated price, it will only be equivalent to one-half of the total debt. Moreover, in this inland area where the economy is extremely panicked, even the land cannot be sold, and the pawnshop is deliberately playing tricks and hesitating. On the one hand, the creditors are forcing and urging the debt, and we cannot live in peace all day long, which makes my family full of sorrow and makes my mother sick! I am really ashamed that I cannot make my mother feel at ease! Now, what I want to ask is: ㈠ The land cannot be sold, and the pawnshop deliberately refuses to buy it, hoping that when we are in extreme difficulty, we will sell it to him cheaply. This landlord's means of exploitation are really hateful! But is it possible to forcibly sell it to the pawnshop? ㈡ The creditor urges the payment of accumulated debts, and the debtor is unable to repay it, and life is almost cut off. How should the debtor deal with it? Is there any provision in the law to sympathize with the debtor's hardship and forgive him? ㈢ Can bankruptcy be declared in law?

Reply: Regarding the three points you asked in your letter, the first point is impossible according to the law; although there is no provision in the law for "sympathizing with the poor and forgiving them" for the second and third points, the law does not force them to repay if the debtors are indeed destitute; as for declaring bankruptcy, no one has ever done it yet. Now it seems that you have to do your best to pay off your debts with all you have (of course, the living expenses that your family should have should be reserved separately). If there is still a shortage, you can write another promissory note, otherwise you can only let the creditor sue, and the court will definitely not force you to create something out of nothing. I hope you can be patient and deal with it without worrying.

Page 11

Girl Dies Suddenly, Awaiting Autopsy 141

Yang Wanfa, a native of Xuzhou, earns his living by rowing a boat in the Huangpu River. His family lives in a shed on the Taoyuanzhai mining land in Pudong. His daughter, Xiaocai, was only thirteen years old, and suddenly died yesterday. Wanfa immediately filed a complaint with the Third District Police Station, accusing his neighbor Zhang Huaide from Huai'an of severely injuring and killing her in an argument. He requested redress. The district approved the complaint and ordered the police to take the defendant to the district for questioning. According to the defendant's reply, he denied committing the crime, stating that the deceased was suffering from a disease, and the plaintiff had invited a fairy (a fortune teller) to the house to diagnose the illness. The fairy took incense ash and gave it to the deceased to swallow, causing her death. Now, the plaintiff has destroyed the fairy's home. The district chief, seeing that both sides had different words, decided that in order to determine the cause of the deceased's death, he summoned the 24th Tu land agent, Xie Along, to request the local court to appoint a prosecutor to come to the scene. The prosecutor found no injuries on the surface of the deceased's body, but Yang still insisted that she was beaten to death by the defendant and that her injuries were internal. The prosecutor then ordered the body to be taken to the court for an autopsy.

Pirates Ruthlessly Rob a Civilian Boat 142

Three Crew Members Killed and Boat Owner's Ear Cut Off

Yong Jihe and several other shops in this port, which handle various merchandise, sugar, groceries, seafood, and foreign goods from Changzhou and Wuxi, loaded the civilian boats Niu Yunfang, Yang Zuolin, and three other boats with goods the day before yesterday for transport. Because they urgently needed to sell the goods, they hired a small towing boat. They agreed with the towing boat to tow them to the Dianshan Lake area, and then each boat would sail on its own way. In the afternoon, after being towed to Dianshan Lake and unmoored, Niu and the other three boats sailed together, while the other two boats went their separate ways. As they sailed near the west end of the lake, before it was dark, four or five pirate boats suddenly sailed towards them, with twenty or thirty pirates on board. They suddenly opened fire, ordering them to stop. The twenty or so people on the three boats, Niu and the other three boats, were still able to resist and continued to sail straight ahead, ordering each crew member to do their best to resist, so that the pirates could not board the boat. Seeing that they did not stop, the pirates immediately raised their sails, chased after them, and opened fire. Three crew members on the three boats were killed, and five or six were injured. The boats were all shot through. Niu's boat was hit with several holes and flooded. At this point, the crew members panicked and were finally caught. The pirates boarded the boat, first asked for the boat owner, and forced him to hand over the silver dollars. All the silver dollars on the three boats were robbed, but because Niu replied that there were no dollars on the boat, he was searched and the pirates were furious. They cut off one of Niu's ears. Then, they continued to loot the goods. Suddenly, they heard the sound of a whistle, and they stopped looting. The pirates returned to their pirate boats and fled. Niu's ear was cut off, and he fainted. The incident was reported to the anti-smuggling patrol boat, which was instructed to investigate, and the boats were sailed to Tagang and docked. The boatmen sent Niu and the three crew members who had been killed by the pirates to the hospital for treatment. Although the three boats of Niu and the others were not completely robbed, the boats were all shot with holes, and Niu's boat suffered the greatest loss. The sugar loaded on the boat was flooded, and the boat could not sail. Yesterday, someone came to Shanghai to report to Yong Jihe and other shops and borrowed silver dollars to buy coffins for the three crew members who had been killed. At the same time, they hired another boat to go there and unload the goods from Niu's boat, and they sent a telegram to the goods companies in Changzhou and Wuxi.

Parents of the Second Jiaotong School Hold a Joint Meeting 144

The Shanghai Second Jiaotong Vocational School of the Ministry of Communications was initially initiated by employees of the Postal Bureau and was later managed by the Ministry of Communications. It has been established for three years, and the number of students has reached more than 200. Although it suffered significant losses during the January 28th Incident, it was soon restored. However, the school is often affected by politics, and the principals have been changed several times, resulting in the school's affairs becoming increasingly stagnant. The parents of the school's students believe that the frequent changes of principals are likely to hinder the school's affairs and affect the children's studies, so there is an organization of the Parents' Association. The purpose is to connect the spirit between the school and the parents, hoping to achieve the effectiveness of both family education and social education, and at the same time, to supervise all school administrative affairs. Yesterday, the association held its second congress, with more than 100 parents attending. The Postal Workers' Union also sent Standing Committee members Lu Keming, Cao Chongye, Wu Tinglun, and Secretary Zhang Kejing. Chairman Meng Fanlin presided over the meeting, and the following proposals were passed: ㈠ The school shall not restrict the number of students; ㈡ Expanding the school buildings; ㈢ Increasing the annual funding; ㈣ Establishing a junior high school; ㈤ The school suffered great losses during the January 28th Incident and should seek special funds to restore it; ㈥ In the future, the school shall not be affected by politics. All of the above proposals were passed and handed over to the Board of Directors for handling. Furthermore, the school's principal, Tong Pingshan, was recently ordered to be transferred. The parents all agreed that the frequent changes of principals are greatly related to their children's education, especially since the term has already changed four times. If he is allowed to be transferred again, the future of the school will become increasingly unsustainable. Moreover, Principal Tong has been handling the school very appropriately since taking office, and although it has not been long, the school's affairs have suddenly progressed. Therefore, it was unanimously agreed to retain him and to petition the Committee on Communications and Employee Affairs to withdraw the order.

Shandong High School Scheduled to Reopen Tomorrow 154

(Jinan Express) The Shandong Provincial Senior High School, which caused the student unrest in Jinan, began identifying students who had repented at all levels today (the 13th). According to the person in charge of the school, the graduating students of the senior third year, classes A and B, had already taken the graduation examination held by the school on the 9th. Forty-five students were approved to graduate and have been reported to the Department of Education for the joint examination. As for the other students, except for 30 students who actively instigated the strike, who will be severely punished, 380 other students have submitted letters of repentance and guarantees and paid various fees after being notified by the school. Only 20-30 students have not submitted them. From today until the 15th, the school will identify those who have submitted letters of repentance by class. After the identification is completed, the school will reopen. The school has now scheduled to reopen on the 18th of this month. If there are special circumstances at that time that prevent the school from reopening as scheduled, it will be postponed to the 19th. The school is taking the identification this time extremely seriously, and the Department of Education is also paying close attention. The Department of Education has sent Inspector Meng Minyan to the school to supervise the examination. It is generally believed that if the identification is not strict enough this time, similar incidents may occur again in the future.

Special Feature

Methods of Hygiene Teaching in Primary and Secondary Schools (Xu En Lecture, Hua Ji) 160

First Type: Child Health Record (Teacher Fills Out)

1. Name, 2. Age, 3. Weight, 4. Weight Gain Rate, 5. Posture, 6. Endurance, 7. Physical Defects: Vision, Trachoma, Hearing, Nutrition, Tonsils, Teeth, Heart, Lungs, Other, 8. Defects Already Corrected, 9. Skin, 10. Infectious Diseases This Year, 11. Vaccinations and Inoculations, 12. Need for Special Teaching Procedures, 13. Academic Performance and Intelligence, 14. Character, 15. Parents' Attitude Towards School Hygiene, 16. Family Situation.

Second Type: Teacher's Assessment of Children's Hygiene Habits

Habit | Opportunity | Practice

1. Games and Exercise, 2. Posture, 3. Eye Protection, 4. Extracurricular Reading, 5. Excessive Number of Bowel Movements, 6. Cleanliness of the Whole Body (Including Clothing) When Going to School, 7. Drinking Water from Own Cup, 8. Using Own Handkerchief, 9. Not Touching Face with Hands and Pencils, 10. Fully Utilizing Sanitary Facilities, 11. Happy and Lively Spirit, 12. Caring for Others, 13. Other.

Third Type: Children's Self-Assessment of Hygiene Habits (Total Score 100)

1. I brush my teeth in the morning (5 points), 2. I have a bowel movement once in the morning (5 points), 3. I wash my face and hands every morning before breakfast (5 points), 4. I always look for cars before crossing the road (5 points), 5. Everything on me is clean when I go to school (5 points), 6. I use my own cup to drink water whether at school or at home (5 points), 7. I don't drink tea (5 points), 8. I drink more than three cups of plain boiled water a day (5 points), 9. I never put the pencil tip in my mouth or on my lips (5 points), 10. I always stand up straight with my chest out (5 points), 11. I wash my hands before meals and after using the toilet (5 points), 12. I always play outdoors for at least one hour a day (5 points), 13. I always chew my food thoroughly before swallowing (5 points), 14. I rarely eat sweets (5 points), 15. I am happy all day long (5 points), 16. I bathe at least once a week (5 points), 17. I always eat some vegetables with my meals every day (5 points), 18. I brush my teeth before going to bed every night (5 points), 19. I always go to bed before 9 o'clock every night (5 points), 20. I always open the window when I sleep (5 points).

Fourth Type: Parents' Assessment of Children's Hygiene Habits

Habit | Opportunity | Practice

1. Wakes up at ○:00 in the morning, goes to bed at ○:00 in the evening (around 10:00 PM), 2. Has a bowel movement once in the morning, 3. Washes face and hands before breakfast, 4. Brushes teeth before breakfast, 5. Eats a substantial breakfast, 6. Eats fresh fruit, 7. Eats an appropriate amount of vegetables, 8. Doesn't drink tea, 9. Doesn't eat sweets, 10. Doesn't eat snacks, 11. Always smiles at home, 12. Doesn't get angry, 13. Plays and exercises outdoors in spare time, 14. Uses own drinking cup and towel, 15. Uses a handkerchief to wipe nose or covers mouth and nose when coughing, 16. Washes hands before meals and after using the toilet, 17. Bathed once this week, 18. Plays with neighboring children after school, 19. Reads for ○ hours in the evening, 20. Brushes teeth after dinner and before bed.

Special Habits

Fifth Type: Hygiene Knowledge and Attitude Test (A Few Examples)

Advanced

A. True or False

1. All mosquitoes can transmit malaria ( ).

B. Recognition Method

1. Vaccination

a. Best in spring ( )

b. Best in autumn ( )

c. Can be done in all seasons ( )

d. Best in winter ( )

Intermediate

A. True or False

1. Vaccination is to prevent smallpox ( ).

B. Fill in the Blank (Basic Hygiene Habits)

1. I bathe at least ······ times every ······.

Teachers can add or subtract from the contents of the five types of forms listed above according to the circumstances. This is just an example. Health education does not emphasize knowledge but habits. These five forms can be used to compare the parents' assessment, the teacher's investigation, and the children's report to determine the children's hygiene status. We can also know what the children are lacking and what they need. In this way, our health education materials will be inexhaustible. However, teachers should never be vague about things they do not know. They should consult doctors to resolve the issues. At the same time, if parents have opinions, they should also ask teachers or doctors to clarify them clearly. Do not harm the children with "probably," "almost," or "carelessly."

Second Step: Choosing Teaching Materials

The new required curriculum standards, curriculum outlines, textbooks, and teaching content can all be organized using the materials from these five types of forms to adapt. When selecting teaching materials, we should pay attention to the following five goals:

1. Adapt to the needs of children: For example, if children have bad teeth, they must find ways to correct them to meet the needs of children.

2. Enhance children's health: When children have bad teeth, teachers should teach children how to protect their teeth and prevent problems.

3. Teaching materials should be scientific: This can be divided into three levels:

(1) Purely scientific: For example, how many cups of boiled water should children drink every day? I think it's not appropriate to specify a certain number of cups. It should be based on the needs of children. Drink boiled water when thirsty, but do not force them to drink five or ten cups. This is truly scientific.

(2) Seemingly scientific: Some people often say that getting cholera vaccinations guarantees that you will not get cholera. Here, "guarantee" is learned, but you get sick. There are strengths and weaknesses in life and physical condition, and good and bad qualities in medicine and environment. How can you "guarantee" that you will not get cholera? Isn't this seemingly scientific but not really scientific?

(3) Unscientific: This is very obvious. Common in the old society, such as using talismans to treat diseases, or seeking divination to treat diseases, etc. The teacher's priority for teaching materials is to ask whether they are scientific or not. After reading the above three points, we know how to make choices more easily.

4. Proportionality of Teaching Material Content: The goal of health education is to cultivate children's habits, intelligence, and attitudes. Low-grade students do not need to know principles because they really don't understand. Therefore, the teaching material on intelligence should be less, and the habit should be supervised and implemented, and cannot be relaxed. Both intelligence and habit should be given equal importance for high-grade students. Now, let's set a ratio below:

Grade | High | Middle | Low

Habit | 40% | 50% | 60%

Intelligence | 40% | 30% | 20%

Attitude | 20% | 20% | 20%

5. Link Teaching Materials of Various Subjects: Which teacher should be in charge of the hygiene subject? Needless to say, the class teacher can take on the job happily. By entrusting this task to the class teacher, the problem of linking teaching materials of various subjects can be easily solved. Item 5 of the Implementation Measures of the Curriculum Standards stipulates: "After the promulgation of these standards, the education bureaus of each county and city should immediately organize a local teaching material collection committee to collect local teaching materials that are actually used in the township based on the operating requirements of each subject in these standards as supplementary teaching materials and submit them to the competent education administration agency for review and approval before adding them to the specific teaching material items." Then, the hygiene subject should also follow the same and do not forget to contact various subjects. For example, the geography subject discusses the nutritional problems of local products, and the natural science subject discusses local animals and plants and leads to sex education issues. There are countless examples like this, and it depends on everyone to do it well.

Third Step: Emphasize Activities

The implementation of hygiene education, especially in lower grades, depends mostly on extracurricular activities, not fixed in class. Of course, teachers should emphasize linking children to do various activities. Teachers should participate in all of the children's actions in a childlike manner. That is, when children go to the toilet, use towels to wipe their eyes, and wipe their noses, etc., teachers must pay attention at any time. The scope of training is very large. All roadsides, sports fields, and test sites are good places for teachers to engage in hygiene activities. The issues of training include: (1) design, (2) demonstration, (3) appreciation, (4) contact, (5) testing, and (6) practice. These teachers should always guide.

Fourth Step: Check Progress

Investigating the progress of children's hygiene habits and attitudes is an indispensable step in hygiene teaching. Rapid and clear progress indicates good teaching. Otherwise, improvements must be made immediately. The progress situation is clear when using these five forms to compare. The tables filled out by the children themselves can give them good stimulation, just like forgetting to brush their teeth. When filling out the form, they will have the reaction of brushing their teeth. Things like this can help children directly.

Special Teaching Methods for Elementary Schools

With the above four steps, the health education problem can be said to be completely solved. Now let's add some special teaching methods for elementary school health education.

(1) Morning Inspection: Everyone should already know this method. This is not a special matter, nor is it a morning meeting. It is one to investigate children's hygiene and implement habits; two to investigate children's cleanliness; three to investigate acute diseases; four to train children to practice self-examination.

(2) Measuring Weight: There is no standard for human weight. The so-called standard is fabricated and unscientific. The purpose of our measuring weight is to see how much the children's body weight has increased, such as one to see the children's progress in development; two to let children understand their own weight progress and arouse interest in health; three if weight does not progress and diseases are discovered, treat them as soon as possible.

(3) Hygiene Self-Government: Many elementary schools have established children's self-government associations. It is a very good thing for children to do their own management. Hygiene education is often completely responsible for teachers and doctors, and children are sitting by and watching. This is wrong. If it is handed over to the children to manage themselves, the efficiency of progress will definitely be easier to see. From now on, we can promote it.

City Education Association Editorial Meeting 162

Monthly Publication Renamed "Shanghai Education Circle"

The Shanghai City Education Association held its second editorial committee meeting yesterday afternoon. Attendees included Huang Zaoxiong, Xu Zeyi, Zheng Baohua, Wu Hanfang, Xu Yaqian, Jiang Wenbao, Ma Zhenbai, and others. Xu Zeyi chaired the meeting, with Huang Zaoxiong as the recorder. The meeting adjourned. The submission guidelines for the publication are recorded as follows: ㈠ Submissions include original and translated works such as essays, research, and investigations related to education. ㈡ Translated texts must include the original text or clearly indicate the corresponding parts of the original text for verification. ㈢ The style of writing is not limited, but all must use modern punctuation. ㈣ Manuscripts must be written on the association's manuscript paper. ㈤ The association reserves the right to modify submissions; those who do not wish to have their work modified must declare this in advance. ㈥ Submissions will not be returned regardless of whether they are published or not. If a return is required, sufficient postage stamps must be included. ㈦ Remuneration: (A) Cash payment of two to five yuan per thousand characters; (B) Copies of the publication. ㈧ If plagiarism or simultaneous submission to multiple publications is discovered, the remuneration will be cancelled. ㈨ Once a submission is published, the copyright belongs to the association.

Zhiren Yong Girls' Middle School Fifth Anniversary 164

Zhiren Yong Girls' Middle School, located at 10 Seymour Road in this city, celebrated its fifth anniversary yesterday. The celebration, initiated by the first-year senior high school students, was held in the auditorium and included performances. The principal, Ms. Xu Renyi, first reported on the school's founding principles and history. She stated that since its establishment, the school has emphasized both academic studies and the combination of Chinese and Western learning, with all courses being of a high standard. While sparing no effort in adopting new European and American methods, the school also emphasizes the promotion of traditional Chinese ethics and morality. To date, graduates have entered various sectors of politics, business, and academia with outstanding achievements, which is a testament to the school's success in the past five years. She then outlined the plans for the next five years: to expand education in rural areas, establish free schools, raise the educational level of farmers, and increase their understanding of the nation. She hopes that women will engage in practical industries, guide the public, improve agricultural tools, and develop production to achieve national salvation through practical efforts, thus dispelling criticism that women receive only vain and superficial education. Afterwards, students performed various programs, including sword dances, singing the fifth anniversary song, "The New Cowherd," "Rubber Man," "School闹," English short plays, and a Chinese opera ("The Detestable Diamond"). The performances were excellent. After the closing ceremony, the first-year senior high students provided tea and refreshments for the teachers and students, who gathered to eat together until the afternoon when the event concluded.

Hongdui is Donghua Association

The Hongdui team in Group 1 of Division B of the Shanghai Basketball Association is organized by the Donghua Football Association. All basketball players are also football players. The purpose is to adjust their interests. The Donghua Association originally intended to participate in both the A and B basketball teams. The Hujiang University team represented Group A. Later, the Hujiang players had to represent the school, so Donghua gave up the idea.

Essays

The Relativity of Snow 176

— Zhan Lu

Snow is full of egalitarian ideas. Looking at the rugged and narrow paths on the mountains, the high and low stone steps are all filled in by it, showing that what it hates most is classism.

Snow is most full of classism, especially distinguishing between the poor and the rich with cold and warmth. It only invades thatched cottages, adding snow to frost for the poor. It does not invade the homes of the wealthy with heavy curtains. Even if it does occasionally invade, it is baked by the electric stove, and it blends in with the warm air in the greenhouse and assimilates.

Snow is pure and flawless. In any competition of pure substances, no one can compete with it. In the end, it always wins the championship in the competition of the pure world.

Snow is capable of hiding dirt and filth. It only adorns the turbid world with a deceiving temporary mask. In fact, it is very dirty. Any filthy thing is under its all-encompassing nature. In the end, it also becomes a filthy thing by following the crowd.

Snow is full of creativity. With just one night's work, the exquisite pavilions and jade buildings that are not easily seen in the human world are all created by it alone. It certainly has creative genius.

Snow is full of imitation. Xie Huilian's "Snow Rhapsody" says, "It becomes a gui (jade tablet) because of the square, and a bi (jade disc) because of the circle." How can it have creative genius? It only inherits and imitates.

Snow has a connection with literary people. Whether new or old literary people, they have a special feeling for it. It also fully provides literary people with convenience in their works.

Snow has a connection with military people. Marching in the snow is a common strategy in war. Li Su's surprise attack on Caizhou on a snowy night is a definite proof that military people have a special feeling for it. It also gives military people rare opportunities for marching.

Snow is······

Snow is······

Modern Artist 177

— Xu Baishi

｜Also a Snapshot｜

Friends, the ones walking happily on the road, carrying a messy little box, a three-legged stool used by shoemakers, and a wooden frame nailed with white cloth, these are artists.

They have a head of messy hair that they intentionally mess up; they may have money, but they intentionally wear such broken and dirty clothes to run outside.

What is this for? It is to be an artist. They usually carry a paint box when they go out, indicating that they are painters. They often go out without wearing socks, the reason being, women can go without wearing socks, why can't men? Besides, I am an artist······.

They don't have to go to school, and they can get up at ten o'clock every day: they often work overtime at night, and what they are working on is writing love letters.

They randomly paint red and green colors on the canvas, as if the canvas is a palette; when people ask them, they say, this is my creation. Moreover, their creative power is very strong. They can produce at least a dozen such paintings every day.

Their lives are very artistic: some wear suits without ties; some wear coats on top and shorts on the bottom; brand-new white leather shoes must be dusted with some gray color before putting them on their feet, and dirty socks are turned over and worn for a few more days; they also put some small patterns on their painting clothes, or draw a kitten or a puppy; or a skull, expressing that they are lamenting youth.

This is the modern artist! The current Chinese artist! Alas, this is what we can see!

Peep Show 178

— Chang Huan

｜Let's Expose One First｜

"The peep show is really fun. For one copper, you can see it three times, just hoping it won't be exposed for a while." What is a peep show? Everything in the world can be said to be a peep show. Because the peep show is all fake, once it is exposed, it is worthless. So I say that everything in the world can be called a peep show, which means that everything in the world is false and deceptive. Readers don't believe it? Please see the examples I give below:

Celibacy

A: "The opposite sex is a poisonous snake and will hinder the progress of my career. Therefore, I will never knowingly commit the crime and embrace celibacy."

B: "Mr. A, didn't you sincerely ask me yesterday to introduce you to someone of the opposite sex? How can you say this again now? That really makes me puzzled."

C: "Mr. B, why do you have to be so serious? | Eating, drinking, and sex, the great desires of man exist therein | Originally, no one in this world is willing to embrace celibacy, right? But because he hasn't found a lover yet, he says this in front of everyone!"

A laughs······ strangely······

B: "Oh! I see!"

Japan's Bitch 179

— Holding a Buddha

｜Many Varieties｜

Prostitution has a long history. Guan Zhong established three hundred female brothels to facilitate merchants. Isn't this the alley of today's brothels? The Analects say: "The people of Qi presented female musicians." Emperor Wu of Han established military brothels for soldiers who did not have wives. By the Song Dynasty, the system of military brothels still existed. Su Dongpo wrote: "Zhou Shao, registered in the military of Hangzhou, collected many rare teas and often competed with Junmo [the style name of Cai Xiang] to win. He also knew how to write poetry. Zirong passed through Hangzhou and treated him to a meal. Shao requested to be removed from the register, and holding a pen, he composed a poem: 'The nest on the ridge is empty, years pass in alarm, I can't bear to look back and dress my feathers; if the snow-clad bird is released from the cage, I will always chant the Prajna Sutra of Avalokitesvara.' Shao was dressed in white at the time, and everyone sighed in admiration." Not only that, but during the Eastern Han Dynasty, Ma Rong set up a crimson curtain. He was a master of classical studies. He lectured students in front and had female musicians behind. From this, it can be said that in ancient times, prostitutes had close relationships with the military, scholars, merchants, and various other circles. Not only in China, but in every country in the East and West, there are prostitutes. Taking Japan as an example, there are many types, so let's briefly list a few.

There are many names for prostitutes. Why are they called "bitches"? A "biao" (婊) refers to a woman outside of the home, meaning she is not the formal wife. Why are they called "changfu" (倡婦)? "Chang" (倡) is interchangeable with "chang" (唱), meaning the female musicians of ancient times. Why are they called "jinu" (妓女)? "Ji" (妓) means skill, like the Japanese "geisha" (藝者) and "maiko" (舞子). There are many names for prostitutes in our country, such as public prostitutes, private prostitutes, "changsan" (長三), "yaoer" (么二), "tangpai" (淌牌), and "yeji" (野雞). It's the same in Japan.

The highest-class prostitutes in Japan are called "geisha" (藝者), like the "qingguanren" (清倌人) of our country in the past. Li Shishi of the Song Dynasty, Dong Xiaowan, Li Xiangjun, Liu Rushi, and Chen Yuanyuan of the Ming Dynasty may be somewhat similar. If you really want to be enchanted, it will cost thousands of yuan, and sometimes it may not even be possible. In Tokyo, places like Nihonbashi, Shinbashi, Yamatashita, Kudanzaka, and Kagurazaka are all their love nests. Their residences are luxurious, and their clothing and decorations are extremely extravagant. Once, a geisha lost a diamond ring worth 18,000 yuan. From this, we can see their extravagance.

Japanese prostitutes are also divided into public and private. Let's talk about the private ones later. The places where the public ones live are called "shōro" (娼樓), like the "qinglou" (青樓), "jiaofang" (教坊), "yaozi" (窰子), and "changmen" (倡門) that we say in our country. The madam is called "tekishō" (敵娼), and also "aite" (相手). The pimp is also called "aite" (相手). The fee for entertainment is called "sekiryō" (席料), and also "yu dai" (湯代). As for the cost, it is calculated by time, about 1.5 to 6 yuan per hour, which is very similar to the tuition fee of a middle school teacher.

There are also "shakufu" (酌婦), like the female waiters in our country, but in Japan, they are hired by restaurants to serve wine to guests. There are also "maiko" (舞子), who are mostly teenage girls, like the dancers in our country's ×× dance troupe and the female performers selling medicine in the streets. They are somewhat different from the dancers in dance halls.

Fiction

Guilty Conscience 180

— By A Thin Red Shrike

After finishing his meals, he had nothing to do every day, so he would chat and joke with the couple at will, without being constrained or polite. When he was happy, he would help them with some trivial household chores, feeding the goldfish, watering the flowers, or keeping track of petty cash; tidying up the furnishings; or else he would go to the bookshelf to find his good companions. Sometimes, when Xiaoman saw that he was too idle and worried that he would get sick from boredom, she would say to him, "You're really lazy; after eating, you don't want to do anything. The parrot on the shelf is almost starving to death. If you continue to be so lazy, I'll send you to herd cows tomorrow. Hey! Be careful..." Or at other times, when he occasionally had a sentimental feeling that stirred up old wounds in his heart, as long as his brow furrowed slightly, as soon as Dongfang Sheng saw it, he would immediately say in a teasing manner, "Haha! What season is it today? This kid's old illness has flared up again. Xiaoman, come, I'll play the zither, you sing a short song, let's all help this kid cure his illness..." In this way, his sorrow and depression were immediately driven away to the land of nowhere by that burst of laughter and the beautiful sound of the zither and songs.

Living such a simple life, ordinary but not monotonous, quiet but not lonely, after only three or four months, he felt as if the world he was in had changed: his body also seemed to have changed, the scars in his heart gradually healed; the courage in life that had been lost gradually revived, until the radiance of his appearance gradually became full. Except for occasionally thinking of his stepmother and his previous circumstances, everything felt happy.

However, in this light and meaningful atmosphere of happiness, there was one thing that often made him feel unhappy. He felt that he had not given Dongfang Sheng any special favors in the past, and it would be difficult to expect appropriate rewards in the future. Could he continue to disturb them like this, and they would never get tired of him? Even if they never got tired of him, his own conscience would not be able to handle it. Once this thought arose, he often couldn't help but say to Dongfang Sheng with embarrassment and uneasiness, "I... I can't possibly be here forever..."

Whenever this happened, before he could finish speaking, Dongfang Sheng would always smile indifferently, as if he had already seen through his thoughts, and immediately stop him from saying, "Little thing, don't say it. Whatever you say, I am willing to listen, but I am not willing to hear the one sentence that you are hiding in your throat right now." Such words were no different from closing the door and bolting it, so he had no choice but to stop in embarrassment. The innocent Xiaoman was especially clever, and whenever he expressed that he felt sorry, she would say with a smile, "We used to dislike our environment very much, feeling it was too dull, so the two of us very much hoped that a child would jump out and liven things up. Unfortunately, we waited for a long time, and finally we were disappointed, which was so unfortunate! Now that you have come, you have added a lot of fun to our boring family. You might as well consider yourself filling the void of that child, wouldn't that be good?" (8)

Shanghai Night Talk 181

— Zhang Ruochun

(1) Avenue Joffre

Avenue Joffre is the most South European-flavored street in the French Concession of Shanghai. It is like a colorful snake, winding from Shanshan Bridge to Route Hoge. Trees are planted on both sides, and in spring, summer, and autumn, the green leaves provide shade, and a verdant color makes people feel a kind of pleasant and comfortable impression.

At dusk, on the smooth sidewalks from Rue de Lu-ban to Avenue Albert, groups of young men and women: black eyes, yellow hair, high noses, red lips, some are fallen White Russian aristocrats, some are retired Khitan politicians, and some are Shanghai modern girls, wandering and strolling, browsing the enchanting window displays of the shops. Lovers, pairs of them, come out of the movie theaters, hand in hand, and go into the cafes. There are also single men, strolling towards the quiet residential areas, looking up at the neat Western-style houses along the road in the hazy night, the colored lights shining through the thin gauze curtains, revealing a corner of the red building. What a poetic and interesting scene this is.

On both sides of Avenue Joffre, there are more White Russian men and women living than French people. Within the French Concession, there are more than 10,000 people who speak Russian, and less than 2,000 who speak French. But these one thousand or so French residents rule over more than 500,000 Chinese people. The lives of the French residents should naturally be excellent and noble.

The White Russian expatriates on Avenue Joffre like to call it Nikolaevskaya ulitsa among themselves. The Jiangbei people who pull rickshaws call it Baochang Road. A small number of Chinese people who like to live the Shanghai nightlife call it "Mystery Street" after the January 28th Incident. The citizens of the French Republic still call it Avenue Joffre.

Every year on July 14th, the French National Day, those who come out to carry lanterns and watch the festivities on Avenue Joffre are almost entirely Chinese. The high-ranking merchants of French foreign firms all hide in the French Club on Rue Mère de Dieu, drinking and reveling all night long. The French soldiers all gather in their own barracks or in the dance hall on Rue Paul Henry to enjoy themselves to the fullest.

More than a decade ago, when welcoming Marshal Joffre to Shanghai, the French Concession was deserted, and everyone competed to "watch Joffre on Avenue Joffre," which was entirely Chinese people supporting the French.

The first magnificent cinema in Shanghai, the Cathay Theatre with its modern architecture, was built on Avenue Joffre. The coolest garden cafe and rooftop cafe are also located on Avenue Joffre. (Unfortunately, this year, "Renaissance" and "Taiga Chinguk" have both closed down one after another.) The most mysterious and exotic midnight dance halls: "Black Eyes" and "New Hawaii" are also on Avenue Joffre. The mysterious dens of massage parlors that used to be lined up in the area of North Sichuan Road and Bazilu, which often aroused the curiosity of the general public, have also moved to Avenue Joffre.

Avenue Joffre is a street full of exotic flavors, the Nikolaevskaya ulitsa of the East, and also the emerging Mystery Street.

The Land of Gentlemen 182

— Menglan

Those with blue eyes and yellow beards call our honorable compatriots "sick men of East Asia."

In fact, this is wrong, no wonder it has aroused strong opposition from our great men and gentlemen, because, not to mention anything else, that term is enough to cause disgust in our great men and gentlemen, although our great men and gentlemen are mostly people who bend over and bow their backs, but you should know that what our great men and gentlemen are most afraid to point out is their weaknesses.

So, in my humble opinion, it should be changed to "Land of Gentlemen," that way, the term is so pleasant to the ear; when the name is correct, the words will be smooth, [although bandit uncles will also "steal the beauty," saying something about "gentlemen on the roof beam," but that is harmless,] even the village schoolteacher in the small village will deeply agree with what I say, saying, "Those who obey me prosper, those who oppose me perish, with this dignified drum and this upright flag, what cannot be overcome!" As for the content, there is no need to delve into it. Our great men and gentlemen only need a pleasant-sounding term. As for whether they are hypocritical gentlemen, true gentlemen, or opium addicts? Blowing wrinkles on a pool of spring water, what does it matter to you?
