Finance 183

Shorts' Swap Spreads Widen Significantly

March Gold Marking Anticipated to Tighten

Shorts Anxious to Cover, Few Longs Available

Spread Widens from Five Cents to 2.5 Taels

Final Stand Between 2.2 and 2.3 Cents

(Market Situation Before and After Swap) Yesterday's gold marking market saw a slight drop in London prices by 0.0625 according to foreign telegrams, yet opened lower. This was due to Bank of America offering long positions at 1.25, and forward silver prices also seeing a slight increase of several cents. Additionally, due to shorts offering swap spreads, the March upturn was expected. Consequently, the March contract opened at 798.5 taels, and the February contract at 799.7 taels, a difference of 1.2 taels, signifying swap listing. Subsequently, shorts were eager to cover, while longs had largely disappeared, pushing the spread higher. The marking price also rose accordingly to 799.5 taels, and the February contract to 800.007 taels. HSBC's listings both rose by 1.25, and the foreign exchange market saw a slight hardening. Coupled with news favorable to the silver market, gold prices gradually fell. Although the Central Bank's spot offerings caused a rebound, prices soon fell again to 793.6 taels, as the bank offered lower half-month US dollars at 1.25 for January and 3.125 for April, with little demand. In the afternoon, the market first rose due to HSBC taking March US dollars at 0.25, and then further to 97 taels as the bank sought to close out contracts for the current month at 28 yuan and May at 3.125, followed by another spot offering from the Central Bank that got up to 8.6 taels. Later, with the foreign exchange market remaining flat, the market closed at 797.3 taels. Initial swap trades saw longs offering seven cents, then five cents, before rising to as high as 2.5 taels, before settling in the 2.2-2.3 tael range. Apart from the Central Bank and some spot dealers holding some positions, few longs were to be seen. The market situation before and after is recorded below.

(Morning Market Tracking the Spread's Fluctuations) The morning opened low, with the March opening at 798.5 taels. Yuankangxiang and Wupin offered terms (Wupin opened at 797.5 taels), gradually dropping to 6.5 taels, as attention focused on the swap market. When the long Hengxing completed its swap, the shorts aggressively increased the spread, and Dadecheng and Hengyu then came to purchase terms, rising to over 8 taels. The bank also opened at this point, with a recent offer of one shilling and eight pence for British exchange and 28 yuan for US dollars, slightly firmer by 0.0625. The bank's private telegram also slightly increased by 0.0625. Dadecheng continued to advance, reaching 9.5 taels. Fushun repeatedly offered, reaching 7.5 taels. As the foreign exchange market slightly hardened, March US dollars at 1.875 could not be sold. Daxing, Yongyuanchun, Yuanmao, Yongdeng, and others offered, retreating to 5.4 taels. Bingxing, Yuanmao, and Yongdeng sold slightly at this point, while Hengyu advanced, improving to 7 taels. HSBC's listings were announced, with British and American exchange both rising by 1.25, slightly declining to 6.5 taels. Yuanheng entered, and prices hovered upwards, with Hengxing also purchasing, reaching 8.5 taels, while Yongfeng offered, dropping to 7.2 taels. During this period, Yuanmao, Yongfuyu sold, while Hengxing and Hengyu advanced. Huabi and Mitsui both took April US dollars at 0.25, rising again to 8.4 taels, fluctuating slightly, but the foreign exchange market changed rapidly. April US dollars at 0.25 suddenly could not be sold, and Hengyu then came to unload, dropping to within 6 taels. Yifeng and Yong also offered, while Qingfa and Yong advanced, holding at 5.5 taels. Hengxing, acting on behalf of the Central Bank, offered at 6.4 taels. Although it continued to offer multiple times after that, the price did not rise, as April US dollars were already trading at 2.125. Zhifengyong also purchased terms at this point, reportedly acting on behalf of Dafeng Heng, resulting in fluctuations around 6 taels. Although April US dollars at 3.125 were also difficult to sell, Yuanchun, Yuankangxiang, and Daxingyong competed to sell, resulting in 3.7 taels, then rising to 4 cents. Finally, the price fell to 93.6 taels due to the Central Bank selling lower half-month US dollars for January at 1.25, closing at this price shortly thereafter. After the close, it was heard that the foreign exchange market saw better transactions, and Yuanheng immediately came to purchase aggressively, reaching 4.5 taels or so, while Wupin had already closed at 3.5 taels.

(Final Result: Down 3.7 Taels) The afternoon market inherited the momentum from the afternoon, opening with a jump of 1.1 taels, at 794.7 taels. Retail investors sold, dropping to 4.1 taels. HSBC took March US dollars at 0.25, rising to 5 taels. Fuyu purchased slightly, reaching 5.2-3 taels. Hongli also advanced to over 6 taels. Dadecheng waited to sell at a limit price of 6.2 taels, resulting in slight fluctuations. However, Fuyu's buying intention was extremely strong, rising to 6.7 taels. Zhifengyong also came to compete for purchases, jumping to 7.2 taels. Yifeng sold, resulting in a slight drop to 6.1 taels. After that, the situation gradually improved, with the bank wanting January US dollars at 28 yuan and May at 3.125. Yongfeng advanced to 7.5 taels. Mitsui took April at 3.125. Yifengyong and Dadecheng advanced to 8 taels. Zhaofengchang purchased terms, reaching 8.6 taels, fluctuating slightly, as retail investors and Wupin sold slightly, then returned to 7.5 taels. Qianchangxiang advanced to over 8 taels. Hengxing, acting on behalf of the Central Bank, advanced, and Dadecheng also purchased, reaching 8.4 taels. After that, although Dadecheng wanted to purchase within 8 taels at a limit price, the foreign exchange market's inability to sell April US dollars at 0.25 led to a downstream trend, hovering around 7.5 taels for a long time. Banks made deals on March 1.875, with other firms wanting to sell but lacking buyers, and prices continued to decline. Hengyu came to sell, resulting in around 6 taels. Daxingyong and Qingfayong then dumped, hovering before seeing 97.8 taels again. At this time, it was close to the close, and little buying or selling was seen. Finally, the market closed at 797.3 taels. Wupin, with aggressive buying, closed at 798.5 taels (double-revealed price). The highest price of the day was 799.5 taels, and the lowest price was 793.6 taels, with a fluctuation of 5.9 taels. As a result, yesterday was down 3.7 taels from the previous weekend.

(Revealed Price Approximately Suppressed by 67 Taels) The revealed price was 864.86 taels due to HSBC's listing of US dollars rising by 1.25 to 27.75 yuan. Based on the closing price, it was approximately 67 taels outside the button. The difference from the previous weekend was minimal. The registered accounts were 796 taels for January and February, and 794 taels for March. Replenishment water was 795 taels in the morning and 798 taels in the afternoon.

(Central Bank Still Offering Spot) Yesterday, a total of about six months' worth of terms were entered, largely done by spot dealers such as Hengxing and Dafeng Heng, with prices from 6 to 7 taels, and 8 taels in the afternoon. Among them, Hengxing's positions were the most.

(On-Market Trading Improved) In summary, Hengxing, Wanxing, Zhifengyong, Bingxing, Yuanheng, Fuchang, Qingfayong, Zhaofengchang, Qianchangxiang, and others were all buyers. Daxingyong, Yongfeng, Yuankangxiang, Yuanmaoyong, Yifengyong, Hengyu, and Fushun were all sellers. Dadecheng, Fuyu, Yuanchun, Hongli, Yifeng, Shunli, and others were first sellers and then buyers. Dalian gang Wanxing advanced over 200 terms in the morning, while Shunli advanced only ten terms. Guang gang Hengxing advanced over 400 terms in the morning, selling a few, and then advanced slightly over 100 in the afternoon. Yifeng's advances and sales were minimal in the morning, and slightly more sales in the afternoon. Wupin's hedging was also a seller.

(Smelting Market Appears More Stagnant) With the Spring Festival approaching, the smelters seemed to have little interest, and the Hakka gang was also stagnant. Although the market saw an increase of 9.5 taels yesterday, it was slightly better than the previous Saturday, due to the swap. Transactions totaled approximately 100 taels. Dafeng Heng sold and then increased to 9.75 taels, which was received by Yingfenghang and others. The silver shop gang sold, with transactions of approximately 200 taels.

(Realistic Account of the Swap) Yesterday morning, before 8 o'clock, dealers had already started the swap. First, shorts offered seven cents, Dadecheng offered, approximately 490 terms, which were taken in by Dalian gang Wanxing and Hengxing. Continuing at five cents, Yifeng then came to swap out long positions, approximately 280 terms. Later, Hengxing swapped out many positions at seven cents, and many shorts were willing to swap, rising to about one tael, still taken in by Hengxing, with Daliancheng and Wupin offering. By this time, the market had opened, and Hengxing had temporarily retreated. Shorts made a strong effort to offer, opening at 1.2 taels, then increasing to 1.7-8 taels, which was taken in by Daxingyong. Hengxing continued to swap out long positions, resulting in mutual price declines to about one tael. After that, longs were scarce. Bingxing came to offer, returning to 1.3 taels, which was taken in by Hengyu. Dadecheng offered Yingfenghang a total of 1.4 taels, Ruikang offered Zhifengyong 1.2 taels, but the numbers were not large. After that, the volume increased, with Wanxing offering Yuanmaoyong 35 terms, reaching 2 taels. Zhaofengchang (acting on behalf of Fuchang) took in 2.3 taels, offered by Qingfayong. Yuanmaoyong then took in 2.5 taels, traded against retail investors. In the afternoon, Hengxing suddenly looked for longs everywhere, offering 2 taels. Bingxing offered Tongfenghang and others 105 terms, at 2.2 taels. It was heard that there was news of spot goods being intercepted en route, coupled with the fact that only spot dealers remained on the long side, and the Central Bank remained inactive, leading to higher spreads. As of the previous Saturday, January's terms totaled 147 terms, and January's total was 17,493 terms.

Zhejiang Anda and Zongfu traded April at 3.125. The Central Bank sold Huabi the lower half of January at 1.25. Huabi took April as high as 3.75. Afternoon closing offers ranged from 1.25 to 3.125. Afternoon trading declined. Citibank first took May at 3.75. Mitsui also scooped up April at 3.125. Zhongfu sold and Huabi took March at 1.875. Citibank advanced and Shanghai plugged February at only 0.0625. The closing offer for January was 28 yuan, 0.0625, February 1.25, March 1.875, and April 2.5, with advance prices adding 0.0625. One American dollar equaled three taels, six cents, zero li, and six hao of silver.

Large Telegram Rises by 0.0625 185

National Society, London, 16th dispatch: Large telegrams have risen by 0.0625 for both near and far terms. The closing price for the near term was sixteen pence and eight-seven-five, and the far term was sixteen pence and nine-three-seven-five. British-American exchange rate opened at three yuan, three cents, five and a half fen.

Banks and Money Shops Exceptionally Busy on Closing Day 186

｜Twofold Business···Closing and Rectifying｜

In recent days, various Chinese financial industries, due to the abolition of the old calendar year-end, have mostly announced their total closure, and the procedures have been more troublesome than usual. The banks were generally closed on Sunday the day before yesterday, and there was no way to collect and resolve accounts. Yesterday, it was necessary to carry out large-scale rectification. Therefore, although the business scene seemed bleak, the rectification situation was indeed vast. Just the settlement of accounts alone was extremely busy. In the money shops, especially, large loans urgently needed to be collected. The busyness of the situation could not be described in words.

Foreign Cents Slightly Lower, Silver Discount Remains the Same 187

"Silver Cents" Yesterday, the foreign cent market price was quite good for bank purchases, but prices were weak, because the sources were plentiful, and the current cash on the market was abundant. The morning and afternoon markets were both at seven cents, one fen, three li, and two hao and a half. As a result, the afternoon market was only one hao and two hu and a half lower than the previous day's afternoon market. Judging from the general trend, there is a possibility of falling but no possibility of rising at present. The "silver discount" opened at two fen in both the morning and afternoon markets. Due to the wide availability of cash, Liu Tou crossed it out all day long.

Copper Dollars Rebound After Slight Drop in Small Silver Coins 188

Jiangnan small silver coins have been lagging behind in recent days, and the market was slightly sluggish yesterday. The morning market was six cents, three fen, four li, and the afternoon market was six cents, three fen, three li. As a result, although the day's market conditions were still three li better than the previous day's afternoon market, the current market situation already felt one li less. One transaction was for 6,500 jiao in the morning market and 3,500 jiao in the afternoon market. Guangdong small silver coins generally trended lower, with the morning market at six cents, two fen, two li and a half, and the afternoon market at six cents, two fen, two li. As a result, the morning and afternoon markets were a total of one li and two hao and a half less than the previous day's morning and afternoon markets. Transactions were made for 115,000 jiao in the morning market and 40,000 jiao in the afternoon market. Copper coins, which have been shrinking sharply in recent days, continued to rise by 1,500 after rebounding by 3,000 the day before yesterday, to 376,500. Transactions were for more than 34,200 strings of cash.

Exceptionally Heavy Clearance at Year's End Under the Abolished Calendar 189

"Silver Funds": Bank clearances seemed busier than usual at the start of the week, and exceptionally busy as the old lunar year's end approached. Chinese merchant clearances totaled 3.67 million to 3.7 million, foreign merchant clearances totaled 3.34 million to 3.4 million, telegraphic transfers exceeded 1.4 million, advances reached 2.56 million, special fund clearances surpassed 5 million, mortgage settlements and new issues totaled 1.7 million, fixed-term clearances were slightly over 5 million, various goods, exchange, taxes, and miscellaneous clearances totaled 9.89 million, warehouse entries were 500,000, warehouse exits were 1.2 million, clearances by native banks and silver firms exceeded 35 million, "quota" clearances exceeded 4.4 million, remittance clearances from various routes exceeded 700,000, cash receipts exceeded 500,000, and settlement funds exceeded 1 million.

Steady Stream of Arrivals; Foreign Exchange Transactions Are Brisk 190

"Foreign Funds": The foreign exchange market was better than usual. Banks were also buying. Exchange and remittance transfers in the early market amounted to 600,050, and in the afternoon market, 1.03 million. Banknotes were 70,000 in the morning and 40,000 in the afternoon. Off-market banknotes were 135,000 in the morning and 75,000 in the afternoon. Bank check transactions were 60,000 in the morning and 65,000 in the afternoon. Bank purchases and sales in the morning mutual market were 950,000, and in the afternoon mutual market, 1.05 million. Foreign customer transactions at various banks amounted to 1.67 million, banknote inflows and outflows were 2.34 million, native bank foreign public bond clearances exceeded 13 million, foreign "quota" clearances exceeded 2.1 million, foreign fund borrowing and lending inflows and outflows exceeded 1.8 million, small native bank transactions were 700,000, customer inflows still totaled 400,000, and outflows were only 100,000. Last week, total arrivals amounted to 1.78 million.

Securities: 19 Series Good Fell by a Yuan Several Jiao 191

Other small declines ranged from a few jiao to eight or nine jiao.

Yesterday's (16th) trading situation at the Chinese Merchants Securities Exchange: Only customs duties were traded in the spot market, opening at 4,000 yuan in the morning; all other securities saw no transactions. The futures market also remained quite sluggish. Market sentiment among buyers and sellers remained quite quiet throughout. The morning session saw approximately 2.8 million in trades, and the afternoon session approximately 2.5 million, for a total of 5.3 million yuan. Of this, salt taxes accounted for over 900,000, and both the consolidated tax and 20 Series customs duties accounted for over 800,000. The rest were mostly around 500,000 to 600,000 yuan. 96 Series customs duties and the like only saw a few tens of thousands of yuan in transactions. As for changes in the prices of various bonds, although the trend continued to be peaceful and there were no major changes between the morning and afternoon sessions, the overall environment made optimism difficult, the situation was unusually chaotic, and with the Lunar New Year approaching and settlement dates drawing near, investors remained cautious and on the sidelines. Buying sentiment was particularly weak, while scattered selling was still not uncommon. Therefore, various prices hovered gradually lower than before. As a result, compared to last week, the 19 Series Good fell by a yuan several jiao, and both the 20 Series and salt taxes also fell by eight or nine jiao each. Other bonds each fell by about half a yuan.

New York Stock Market Sluggish 192

A report from the New F丰 Foreign Firm: Last Saturday (14th), the New York stock market was unusually sluggish. The market situation improved slightly due to a good earnings report from the Reynolds Tobacco Company. In the week from January 1st to 7th, the total number of railroad freight cars was 435,652, an increase of 28,873 compared to the previous week, but a decrease of 136,026 compared to the same period last year. The half-day trading volume was 361,000 shares. This recent stock market rise is still largely based on hope and psychological factors. With the start of a new year, people generally hope that industry and commerce can gradually recover, and they especially hope that the next administration can promote this recovery. Other factors, such as rumors that the government will improve the railroad situation and provide relief to rural areas, have also temporarily excited the stock market. However, observing the current situation, it seems to be showing signs of exhaustion. The Dow Jones indices for the 14th are listed below:

Lackluster Cotton Yarn Market 193

Busy Year-End, Slack Trading, Short Positions Appear

The yarn market is extremely lackluster, with no signs of recovery. As the abolished lunar year-end approaches, various parties are busy settling accounts, and the scope of business is shrinking, resulting in very quiet trading and minimal fluctuations. Short positions occasionally appear, but some are optimistic about overseas cotton yarn being more stable and are considering higher prices for goods in distant months next year. The war clouds looming over the Northeast have significantly impacted the financial situation.

(Thin Upward and Downward Momentum in the Human Standard) The human standard (Ren Biao) market opened with American cotton being flat and weak, and gold prices trending lower, leading to weaker sentiment. Prices for all months fell by one, two, or four qian. In the afternoon, although actual demand was sluggish, Chang Feng Hao purchased 1,300 bales, tightening market sentiment, and prices for all months rose by one, two, or four qian. The total trading volume for the day was 9,900 bales. Sales included 850 bales from Sen Kang, 350 bales from Shen Ji, 650 bales from Yuan Da, and 500 bales from Chun Ji. Purchases included 1,350 bales from Chang Feng, 650 bales from Xin Cheng, and 300 bales from Da Chang. The closing prices are listed below:

Factory Empty; Compensation for This Month's Cotton 194

| Distant Futures Also Pick Up Slightly |

The cotton market started weak but then strengthened. American cotton was flat, and gold prices continued to decline, causing sentiment to weaken slightly. However, a certain factory compensated for some of its short positions for this month, stabilizing market sentiment, and distant futures rose slightly. Nevertheless, trading remained light. Most on the market are bullish, citing continuous rain and mold, and frozen inland rivers making transportation difficult.

(Stable Zheng Standard) The Zheng Standard market opened weak, following foreign cotton, with trading light. Prices for all months fell by five fen to one and a half qian. In the afternoon, major short sellers compensated for this month's positions, pulling up distant futures. Prices for all months rose by one qian to one and a half qian. The total trading volume for the day was 26,800 dan. Sales included 2,600 dan from Chun Ji, 1,200 dan from Sui Long, 1,300 dan from Yuan Da, and 800 dan from Yuan Da, 700 dan from Ji Feng. English and Indian Cotton Industry Weekly News 195

(Mumbai) Market conditions were firm last week. News from New York was unfavorable. Hedging increased due to an influx of Indian arrivals. Export inquiries were poor, and Japan was also indifferent. In the next two to three weeks, shipments are expected to be healthy, but whether this will offset the influx is questionable, as the weather is quite favorable for cotton picking. Interpretations of American cotton measures varied in this market. However, the basis for optimism lies not in facts but in faith. (Liverpool) Spot sales were brisk last week. Futures trading was flat. Market conditions were firm. There was hedging on the weekend, mostly selling old cotton and buying new cotton. Egyptian cotton was weak due to unfavorable news from Alexandria.

Grains: Rice Market Downriver Weakens Due to Rain 196

(South Shanghai) Yesterday, due to rain, only sixty-odd boats arrived. Wholesale and retail sales were stagnant, causing the market to fall. Prices for rice from Suzhou and Tongbang fell by three or four jiao. Prices for Nan Gang Qing Jiao, Changbang, and other white polished and thin rice varieties successively decreased by two or three jiao. However, Du Yang Jian rice, lacking stock, was able to hold its ground, varying in price to suit the market, and so was slightly weaker.

(North Shanghai) Yesterday, thirty-odd boats arrived from downriver. Early market retail sales of white polished rice were slightly better, but in the afternoon, shop sales were slow, causing market conditions to fall by two jiao. Due to continuous rain, little was sold. Thin rice and early rice arrivals continued, with retail sales being even, and market conditions decreased by two or three jiao. Arrival and sales of Yangbu Jian were even, and the market trend was stable. High-quality Du Jian rice was scarce, with mid-grade rice slightly available, but turnover was stagnant, and prices were slightly out of line. Although arrivals of variable yin rice were not strong, retail sales were normal, and prices were down by two or three jiao.

Foreign Rice Orders Are Again Viable 197

Customer Indica Sales Are Sluggish and Expected to Remain Flat

Yesterday's customer indica market conditions were affected by the influx of Du rice from downriver and falling prices. Importers were cautious, intending to lower prices, while cargo owners, due to high costs and limited stock, were unwilling to sell at lower prices. Therefore, Xiang province indica and other rice varieties were mostly held back from sale. In the afternoon, the Quanzhou group sold 450 bags of high-quality Ganwan rice, and because the Ganwan rice stock was even scarcer, prices were able to hold.

The foreign rice market has been quiet for a long time, with a remaining stock of more than 300,000 bags, but all of it is in the hands of foreign merchants who are unwilling to sell. However, foreign telegrams reported small gains. Yesterday, Yuan Li Foreign Firm telegraphed a price of 4 taels, 3 qian and 5 fen for Saigon rice number 1 for March and April shipments, which translates to only about 9.2 yuan in the Shanghai market. Since the current spot price in the Shanghai market is 9.5 yuan, there is a possibility that it is again viable. However, rice merchants have suffered greatly from foreign rice in the past two years, and even if it is viable, they are afraid to make inquiries, having been burned before.

Flour and Wheat Fall in Tandem Amid Continuous Price Drops in Foreign Wheat 198

Fu Xin Fixed Australian Wheat at 1.5 Ships for Only 3 Taels, 6 Qian and 7 Fen

The flour market is generally weak and spiritless. Foreign wheat quotations continue to fall by about two jiao. Sentiment regarding near and distant futures has now also changed. Although spot goods are still scarce this month, customer groups are selling back due to the completion of shipments. Distant months have seen consecutive transactions for foreign wheat in very large quantities (one shipment of 9,000 tons was traded last Saturday, with a March shipment price of 3 taels and 7 qian). Yesterday, it was reported that Fu Xin had again fixed Australian wheat at 1.5 ships for March shipment, with the price reduced to 3 taels, 6 qian and 7 fen. The dumping of foreign wheat continues as before, causing sentiment to become unsettled again. Additionally, due to the Lunar New Year, buyers are becoming quiet, making the market even more desolate. As a result, this month's futures fell by one fen and a half compared to the previous week, February futures fell by one fen and three li, March futures fell by one fen and two and a half li, April futures fell by one fen and a half, May futures fell by one fen and two and a half li, and June futures fell by one fen and seven and a half li.

The wheat market unanimously showed a sharp decline. With foreign wheat quotations continuing to fall by two jiao, and with general floating, the market is naturally weak and soft. The degree of decline in each month varies, with March being the most affected. This month's futures are weaker because of recent foreign wheat imports, and traders are preparing to take delivery (currently berthed at buoys 3 and 4). Distant futures have seen continuous foreign wheat transactions, with prices gradually falling. These factors easily affect the psychology of bulls, so opening prices do not show any recovery, and subsequent actions, such as mass selling, could easily cause further fluctuations. As a result, this month's futures were slightly better by one fen, February futures fell by three fen, March futures fell by five fen, and April futures fell by five fen. According to the Chicago wheat report on the 14th, wheat fell by 0.5 to 0.75 fen due to a weak Liverpool market and poor export demand. 20 million bushels were traded on the 13th. Yellow Beans Stable, Oil Market Remains Tight 199

The yellow bean market is trending stable, with slight trading in high-quality beans. Turnover of middle-quality beans is stagnant. Currently, both buyers and sellers are not in a hurry, so market conditions are unchanged. Inland grain mills bought three truckloads of Dalian beans, and factories bought one truckload of Zhengyangguan beans, and one truckload each of Linhuaiguan and Tancheng beans. The Wentai group bought 200 bags of Pudong Du beans, and another 170 bags were bought by Muji Street. The oil market remains tight, and Yutai and Tongtai imported 150 pieces of raw oil, with prices at 13 taels and 3 qian.

Silk and Tea: 540 Pieces of Sichuan Silk Arrive in Shanghai 200

Since the outbreak of war, the source of Sichuan silk had been cut off. Now that Sichuan Province has been pacified, merchants are shipping the accumulated yellow silk from the production areas to Shanghai one after another. Last week, Yangtze River steamers from Hankou transported a total of 540 pieces of Sichuan factory silk and coarse yellow silk.

Slight Clearance of Foreign Estate Tea 201

Yesterday, various European estates were packing and shipping out the large batch of Zhenmei tea purchased last week, awaiting overseas telegrams. Only Tongfu, Jinlong, Yingfa, and other firms bought a total of 402 boxes of Zhenmei, Needle Tea, and Pearl Tea, with no price fluctuations. There were no transactions for Wuyuan Gongse Zhenmei throughout the city.

Coal: Tense Situation in Shimenzhai Warfare 202

Sources of Changcheng and Liujiang Coal Cut Off

Weak Inventories... Market Prices Soar

Recently, the fighting in Shimenzhai has been fierce, and the sources of Changcheng and Liujiang coal have suddenly been cut off. Sea coal inventory can only supply for half a month, causing panic in the coal industry, resulting in soaring prices. Yesterday, the company had no spot goods for sale, and wholesale prices among traders in the market soared further. In particular, Liujiang lump coal was called up to around 15 taels per ton from 13 taels, 7 qian and 5 fen, and small lump coal was also called up to 12 taels. Changcheng white coal also rose by about two taels, and now sells for 16 taels, 5 qian per ton.

Free Talk

Master and Apprentice (2) 227

-- Shou Juan

The master took a sip of white spirits, his chatterbox opened; "We poor people just need to be patient, and honest when doing things, 'Heaven will not disappoint those who suffer!' You'll never have to worry about starving to death! Da Mao, you don't know! I had it even harder than you when I was a kid! My dad died when I was six! My mom died when I was ten! I was left with nothing, no relatives or friends, and there wasn't a grain of food left in the house! Luckily, Uncle Wang next door, took pity on me and asked me to look after his cows, so I lived at his house for two or three years. When I was thirteen, Uncle Wang recommended me to the Maochang blacksmith shop in town to be an apprentice. That's how I learned this hard trade! Later, the master saw that I was willing to endure hardship! That I had a good heart! So he married his daughter to me! But after a few years, Maochang closed down because business was slow. And in that year, Azhen's mother also died! That year must have been when I was down on my luck! I was so disheartened that I didn't want to do anything. But in the end, I felt so sorry for Azhen, so I worked as a day laborer every day! After many years of hard work, I finally saved up a little money, and painstakingly opened this shop. Now, at least everyone has enough to eat! Seeing Azhen growing up to be pleasing to the eye, I feel content!"

The master took another sip of white spirits, and looked at his daughter. His daughter remained silent, obediently sitting by the stove to start the fire. The master's gaze turned to my face.

"It's just that I don't have a son; if Da Mao is good, and works hard, I'll marry Azhen to you. You two would be a good match!"

I was so happy that I almost cut my finger with the kitchen knife. I looked at Azhen, who was blushing and lowering her head.

"What are you smiling about!"

My heart is really smiling!

One morning, the master had to go to town. He said that recently there had been floods in various rural areas, soldiers were fighting, and they were constantly passing through. The servants nearby were either dead or gone, and all the fields were abandoned. The big pile of scythes, hoes, sickles, ······ that we made in the shop every autumn had no sales at all today. So the master was worried and wanted to go to town himself to hawk them.

After the master left, my apprentice sister and I were playing with coppers in the house.

I flicked my copper with my thumb and it rolled straight to the threshold. Azhen didn't pay attention, and it landed flat, bouncing only a few inches away with a "slap".

"It's crooked! It doesn't count! It doesn't count!" I was about to use my copper to hit hers, but Azhen picked up her copper and said coquettishly, "I'm cheating! I won't do it," and I got angry and started to walk out.

"Come on! Come on!" Azhen hurriedly waved her hand.

"Can you cheat from far away?"

"I won't cheat anymore!"

I came back in, Azhen's cheeks were bulging and red! Her two eyes were staring straight into my heart.

"Shame on you! Winning your own family's money!"

The sun shone into our shop. The master came back, followed by a middle-aged man in a melon-shaped cap and a leather jacket with a turned-up collar.

The master said, "This is Sixth Granduncle from Master Chun's house. Master Chun specifically asked him to come to our house to choose some furniture for the wedding! Da Mao! Pour Granduncle some tea!"

I poured a cup of tea and handed it to the young man with both hands. But the young man didn't even look at me straight. His eyes were fixed on Azhen, darting around. (To be continued)

Launching a National Revolutionary War 228

-- Ziguzi

Everyone knows that since the September 18th Incident, the Japanese imperialists have intensified their aggression against our country, with the unprecedented global economic panic as its "driving force." Only the muddleheaded and ignorant believe that it is due to the rash actions of a few Japanese warlords or an accidental unfortunate event. Everyone knows that for the Japanese imperialists' acts of aggression, we have no other way to go except to mobilize the whole country to seek self-defense and self-salvation through our own efforts. Only the timid and cowardly believe that non-resistance can win the sympathy of the world and strive for final victory. The fact is as clear as iron: Since the September 18th Incident, Japan's aggression has only increased, and our policy of non-resistance is just sitting and waiting to be slaughtered, closing our eyes and waiting for death. If we don't wake up now, when will we?

Moreover, the recent public opinion of the great powers towards Japan is even more clearly in support of Japan. The British government's propaganda machine said: "Our former allies are sacrificing for the world and preparing for a decisive battle with the Soviet Union. We should help with the affairs of North China, not interfere." The French media is just busy declaring that the "Franco-Japanese Alliance" and the "Franco-Japanese Secret Agreement" are not facts, and does not comment on the substance of the matter. Italy said it even better: "Who cares, let the Orientals kill each other for a while." This is the "public opinion" of the world, and it is also the harvest of our appeals and pleas since the September 18th Incident. The facts have already clearly pointed out: Under the impact of the global economic panic, in order to struggle for its last destiny, the steps of the imperialists have been consistent. Although their mutual contradictions are also increasingly sharpened, they will always stand on the same front with regard to "another kind of struggle" and the slaughter of weak nations.

Therefore, at present, we must never beg for mercy from the devil again, and we must never sit and wait for death any longer. We can only launch a national revolutionary war and fight to the death against the powerful enemy for our own future and the future of the world. We should not think that this is an echoing sound from the sea, because we also have our own "united front."

New Spring 229

-- Zhou Lengjia

Silently, I accepted this New Spring of 1933.

Outside the Guanzhong, imperialists are wantonly carrying out massacres, guns are booming, and blood is splashing.

Shanghai, this paradise built on hell, is still decadent and extravagant, a world of prosperity.

Many people are shouting about entertainment to save the country, and many people are busy dancing and selecting flowers.

At the Tianchan Stage, Dr. Mei is performing, and the audience is packed.

On North Sichuan Road, in the rows of dance halls, harmonious and pleasant jazz music is playing vigorously; a large group of young people, with their arms around the waists of the dancers, are dancing the foxtrot, tango, and waltz to the rhythm of the music.

Movie theaters are opening their big mouths, and fashionable men and women are flocking in like bees. Large movie advertisements are plastered everywhere on the walls: a foreign girl kicks up a bare leg. Under the bare leg, five big characters, "Crazy Saturday."

Streetcars, ding! ding! ding! Cars, woo! woo! woo! The people sitting in the cars, the men with rosy faces, the women delicate and charming, laugh intoxicatingly.

The wild wind is blowing, like a ghost calling.

An old news vendor, holding up his arm high, shouts out a thunderclap with all his might. "Extra! Want to buy it? Japanese soldiers have entered Shanhaiguan, and 1,800 Chinese have died."

The thunderbolt flies straight into the sky, and when it hits the sky, it falls down, straight into everyone's heart.

The stores, the banners for big sales cover the space. Copper drums, dong! dong! tong! Foreign horns, beep! beep! Blowing and beating, playing together: "The first month is the New Spring..."

The wireless telephone is broadcasting, ji li gu lu, Lu hee hee, Qin ha ha.

An old woman in rags is staring intently at a woman in a fur coat.

Soviet Theater 230

-- Zhao Mingyi

Soviet theater is inseparable from socialist construction. In other words, theater in the Soviet Union is also a part of socialist construction.

Before the First Five-Year Plan, the content of Soviet theater was the use of very stimulating, destructive themes in scripts. At that time, the main task of theater was to clearly point out the importance of the revolution for the liberation of the proletariat; but from the beginning of the Five-Year Plan, the proletariat itself rose up to create new forms of art. Before, they were just passive spectators, but now they have become active participants in artistic creation.

Looking at the directory of theater during the implementation of the First Five-Year Plan, we find that many of them take the current Five-Year Plan of a particular industrial or cultural sector as their theme, to describe their backwardness in production, lack of technology, and the sabotage of the liquidationists, and how to achieve or exceed the planned success. In particular, the development of heavy industry, the collectivization of agriculture, and the eradication of illiteracy, theater undertook its combat mission.

Now let us take an example to illustrate. On the Soviet stage, the following story was once performed.

When the curtain opens, the stage is a barren land, and the farmers are cultivating it with old-fashioned farm tools. Some of them are complaining, so a Trotskyist propagandizes to them that it is absolutely impossible to implement socialism in agriculture. As a result, many people are shaken and become pessimistic. The young shock brigade members among these farmers have advocated using tractors to cultivate the land from the beginning, but the stubborn guys in general do not believe in the truth of this reasoning no matter what. At this time, the young people propose to borrow tractors from the government. When everyone is disappointed, this proposal is reluctantly passed.

Then the stage scene changes, and a huge tractor crosses the stage, and the new land is cultivated. At the end, a field of golden wheat is presented in front of the audience, and everyone cheers. People have won, hearts have won, and socialist construction can proceed.

○ ○ ○ ○ ○

The Five-Year Plan also had a special product in Soviet theater, namely Tram (Youth Workers' Theater Troupe). Tram is different from the past in terms of the form and content of theater, and it is also completely different in Idevoroki. It grasps dialectical materialism as the basis of its activities. That is to say, all theatrical activities must be material and dialectical in development. Therefore, they were able to directly help the work of "completing the Five-Year Plan in four years" and overcome many important difficulties in production.

Now the Second Five-Year Plan has begun, and in the meantime, the main goals of Soviet theater are: 1. Eliminate the imbalance and opposition between cities and villages, establish a large number of rural theaters, organize more shock theater troupes, and AgitProp; 2. Bring the culture of many backward nations to the highest level; 3. Thoroughly eliminate the remnants of capitalism and eliminate the relationship of exploitation of people by people. This is of course consistent with the overall plan.

Long Creation

The Crossroads of Era and Love (Continued) 231

— Zhang Ziping

No matter what, it's hard to deny that there is love between the two of them. If this love is allowed to deepen, it is extremely dangerous. No matter what, even if not for myself, I must keep Peizhu pure. The blood in my body is absolutely pure! Except for Peizhu, the noble and beautiful object of my love, my purity must not be released for other women. Even if Zhuo Shuhua, that pure and chaste woman, comes to challenge me, I must actively resist, and resist for a long time! Moreover, towards Hezi, who is of a different race, and my father's concubine, and a middle-aged woman who is almost thirty years old, even if I cannot strictly defend my country, I cannot completely remove the barriers. If I still harbor this ignoble thought, then I am a useless degenerate! I am a dignified Chinese man, and I should firmly uphold the reputation of the descendants of the Yellow Emperor!······

Thinking of this, Haiquan unconsciously clenched his fists and hammered his head three times.

"Even if she weren't my father's concubine, even if she weren't a middle-aged woman, even if she were like that beautiful Japanese girl, I should still maintain the status of a great Chinese citizen, and shouldn't fall so easily, to be looked down upon by the Japanese devils!······"

As he was lost in thought, Madam Hezi, even more beautifully made up than before, and wearing her favorite fashionable clothes, walked into his room with a smile. As soon as Haiquan saw her, his heart pounded again, and the "Chinese soul" he had just mustered seemed to melt away in Madam Hezi's beautiful appearance.

"Oh my, hasn't the maid brought breakfast yet?"

She asked him with a smile. At first, she was serious, but after saying that, she smiled again. As soon as he saw her smile, his whole body seemed to soften.

"Useless! I'm still useless! My spirit is really weak!"

Before long, the maid brought two servings of breakfast.

"From this morning on, I will accompany Mr. Lin to eat every meal. Mr. Lin is not allowed to eat outside!"

She said coquettishly.

"What about them?"

Haiquan was still concerned about that Japanese man and that Japanese girl.

"Never mind them! Tell the maid to send it to them!"

Shen Bao Local Supplement

Essays

Deception and Exploitation 232

— Zhen Liu

"Deception, exploitation," these four words are sometimes used by foreigners for international political competition, to seek the interests of one country. The Chinese have always used them internally to seek personal gain. By comparison, there is a world of difference! We should remember that during the European War, Wilson said, "Breaking the German dream of unifying the world by force is to seek peace for the world and liberation for small and weak nations." These beautiful words stirred the hearts of small and weak nations, so they believed that Wilson's words were true. Therefore, each small and weak nation resolutely and sincerely joined the Allied front and fought against Germany. As a result, Germany was defeated, and the European War ended. Not only did the victorious imperialists not grant self-determination and autonomy to the small and weak nations, but they also formed the League of Nations as a base camp for imperialism to control the small and weak nations, redistribute spoils, and subjugate them again, so that they would forever be under their iron hooves, without a chance to rise up. It can be seen that the imperialists are all standing in the position of a country's interests, and there is no doubt that they are deceiving and exploiting small and weak nations.

Let us further observe. From the September 18th Incident to the present, it has been more than a year. The violent Japanese invasion is still pressing towards the interior of our country. How can the League of Nations have the determination to sanction the violent Japanese? Doesn't the League of Nations superficially invite the United States and Russia to attend and discuss the Sino-Japanese issue? In essence, it is using the United States and Russia's attendance at the League of Nations as an expression of peace in the Far East, invisibly dispelling the United States and Russia's strategy of attacking Japan, and invisibly deceiving the Chinese government's clever plan. However, our great officials are still singing merrily in leaky boats, engaging in lofty discussions to deceive the national public and exploiting each other to consolidate their personal positions. They are just holding positions without doing any work, putting the country aside. "When those in authority lose their way, the people will scatter." This has made China a complete mess, beyond repair. The reason is that few of us are dedicated to doing things, and many are dedicated to being officials. Few are seeking the interests of the public, and many are exploiting the public. Those above act like those below, and this has become a common practice. They compete for power and seek to satisfy their personal hopes of promotion and wealth, resulting in a militarized and bureaucratic China, a deceptive and hypocritical society, where everyone is cheating and deceiving each other, and engaging in intrigue. This is simply digging one's own grave and inviting one's own destruction.

However, what is past is gone, but what is to come can be pursued. From now on, we should wash our faces and renew our hearts, strive to create a genuine society, eliminate the evils of deception and exploitation, and mold everyone to have a mentality of forgetting one's family for the sake of the country, and forgetting one's self for the sake of the public, and to have the concept of sacrificing one's family to relieve the country's difficulties. Even if the country reaches a point of no return, we must work together to overcome difficulties, turn danger into safety, and reach the shore of salvation. I hope we will all "think thrice"!

Namo Amitabha, please recite it one thousand times or one hundred times or ten times, and you will receive ten kinds of merits in this life.

Mr. Ye Jingfeng: I have forgotten your address and cannot send you a letter. Please come to the Shen Bao office for a talk after seeing this notice. Yao Zichu.

Literature and Art

Airplane Flight 233

— Zhuo Han

Lie Zi once rode the wind, and Lu Ban ascended wooden birds. The past is difficult to verify in history, but today people's skills have just begun. Light cars with silver wings, initially circling on the ground, slowly rising into the sky, with a view of mountains and rivers becoming small. In an instant, thousands of miles, wandering in all directions, pushing through the clouds to the ninth heaven, the sky is high and the white sun is bright. There are also those that fly on the water, surging through the waves, so agile. I am amazed by the wonders of creation, but I only see the ingenuity of people's minds. It is a pity that new weapons are used to disturb mediocre people. The world competes to strengthen their armies, sharpening their fangs and claws. The offensive is launched from the ninth heaven, overlooking everything clearly. Thousands of pounds of sulfur and fire are thrown, and dangerous buildings burn on the bursting ground. Imagining aerial battles, long smoke covers the castles. Thousands of groups of chaotic crows rise, with good skills both above and below. Machine guns fire with a "pa-pa" sound, and flying cannons sweep through the air. There are also those who run out of ammunition and resort to the ram's attack. Broken heads and folded wings, falling like rain on the trees. Flesh and blood fall like mush, and the smoke of burning bodies curls up. I hope to become powder, and the territory will be preserved. Alas, my country is ill, and its plans are sparse and preparations are few. Shanghai is still scorched earth, and Yanyun is about to become a swamp. I heard that aerial defenses are being built, and it is better to mend the fold early.

Science

Talking about Milk 234

— Xin

We have long recognized "milk" as a nutritious food, especially Europeans and Americans, who consume it almost every day. It is generally divided into three types: fresh milk, canned condensed milk, and powdered milk. Now, I will describe them separately:

Fresh Milk

Composition of Milk: To know the relationship between milk and human nutrition, we must first understand its composition. Fresh milk is a white liquid obtained directly from the udders of dairy cows. Its specific gravity is about 1.033. It contains 84% water, 4% butter, 5% casein, and 5% lactose. In addition, it also contains a small amount of inorganic salts (such as calcium phosphate), vitamins A and D, and several yeasts that are beneficial to human digestion, such as trypsin, pepsin, and lipase. Milk also contains dissolved gases (such as hydrogen and nitrogen).

The Relationship Between Milk and Human Nutrition: The nutrients we need in food are nothing more than fats, carbohydrates, proteins, and indispensable vitamins. Since we know the composition of milk as above, we immediately recognize milk as a nutritious substance. Because almost all the nutrients needed by the human body are present in milk: butter for fats, lactose for carbohydrates, casein for proteins, and two kinds of vitamins, as well as calcium phosphate, which is important for bones. Furthermore, much of what we eat can be digested and absorbed by the body with the help of corresponding enzymes. Lipase can digest fats. In the acidic environment of the stomach, pepsin helps to digest proteins into amino acids, which can then be absorbed by the intestines. Trypsin can also help to digest proteins, but without the need for hydrochloric acid. Looking at the above points, it is undeniable that milk is considered to be quite nutritious.

Milk that has been exposed to the air for a long time will turn sour, and at the same time, the oxygen will coagulate into lumps due to the effect of acidity. This is because an enzyme in the air, called lactic ferment, causes the lactose to oxidize into lactic acid. Moreover, there are many microorganisms in the air, and milk is very suitable for the growth of bacteria, so it spoils easily.

Since milk contains yeast and vitamins, it should not be heated to too high a temperature when consumed, otherwise, the vitamins and yeast it contains will be destroyed, and its nutritional value will undoubtedly be reduced. However, if the milk contains bacteria, it should be boiled to prevent infection.

Sterilized Milk: Since milk is directly consumed, its unsanitary condition can transmit diseases. We know that if the cows that supply milk are sick, their milk often contains pathogens. The most common and dangerous is Mycobacterium tuberculosis. More than half of the cows have this disease. Therefore, to avoid this danger, milk is sterilized before being sold in dairy farms. As a result, "A" milk, sterilized milk, Pasteurized milk, etc., are commonly seen on the market. Pasteurized milk is sterilized using Pasteur's high-pressure steam sterilization method. "A" milk is sterilized milk that has been inspected by the Public Works Department as superior milk. There are two sterilization methods. One is high-pressure steam sterilization, in which milk is placed in a sterilizing pot and high-pressure steam is passed through it. The other sterilization method is low-pressure sterilization. In this method, milk is sterilized in a low-pressure environment. In other words, because the air pressure is reduced, it can be sterilized without using high temperature, so there is little change to the inherent components of milk.

Condensed Milk

Ordinary condensed milk is mostly a yellowish-white viscous substance, packaged in cans, and tastes very sweet. Its production method is to concentrate fresh milk with heat or steam, and add sucrose to increase the sweetness. Because the amount of water evaporated is not fixed, its composition cannot be accurately calculated. The water content in ordinary condensed milk is only 26%, and the percentage of other components is therefore increased. Butter is 95%, casein is 10%, lactose is 16%, and sucrose is about 04%. Therefore, when drinking condensed milk, it must be mixed with water so that its composition is the same as fresh milk.

Condensed milk is convenient for use and preservation, especially for travelers. However, because it is concentrated using heat, the vitamins and beneficial yeast in it have already disappeared. Furthermore, if the metal in the can containing this condensed milk contains poisonous substances such as lead, it can make the condensed milk unsuitable for hygiene.

Powdered Milk

Powdered milk is widely used because it is easy to carry. The production method of powdered milk is to evaporate fresh milk to dryness at a relatively low temperature, which takes a long time. The components of powdered milk are of course more abundant than those contained in condensed milk. However, to obtain a beautiful, smooth, light, and dry powdered milk, part or all of the butter is often removed to avoid the powdered milk from clumping together, so its composition is not fixed. Therefore, its nutritional value cannot be determined, and preservatives are often added to powdered milk to prevent fermentation and spoilage. It should be known that no matter what kind of preservative is not suitable for the human body. Therefore, users of powdered milk must be cautious.

Approaching the Enemy (Chinese Troops) 235

— Wen

Sorghum 236

— Chen Zhou

It was late at night, and the snow was still falling non-stop, piling up more than three inches thick in the courtyard, shining white. The crazy north wind was raging, rattling the outer windows. A stove was burning in the house, and the Yuan Shu family was sitting around the stove, talking about urgent news about the war. A kettle on the stove was boiling vigorously, and Yuan Shu removed the lid of the kettle.

"Dad! Many volunteer soldiers have arrived here again today!" Yuan Shu's son Lang said, already eighteen years old.

"Knock! Knock! Knock!" Someone knocked on the door, the servant opened the door, and a person walked in.

"I am here on behalf of the regiment commander. I request that you allow the sorghum on the willow tree pier not to be cut down, in order to facilitate military operations."

"Please sit down, and we can talk," Yuan Shu personally brought a stool for the person to sit on. "It's okay not to cut it down, but how many comrades do you have here now?"

"Not many, only about three hundred. We are here urgently to resist the enemy on the orders of our superiors, so we lack bullets and food. Please help us!"

"Yes! What this brother said is right. We must do it for the country and for ourselves! Dad! Seeing the enemy attacking here, how can our volunteer soldiers resist without bullets and food! Our happy family is built on the country. If the country dies, our happy family will also be gone, and our flesh and blood will be separated... Moreover, there is the stinky name and shame of being slaves of a conquered nation... Dad! Saving the country is saving ourselves! Naturally, we can't talk about sacrificing our family to relieve the country's difficulties, but we must do our best! Dad! You contribute money, and I contribute effort. I will go with this brother and join the volunteer army to kill all those unreasonable enemies!"

"What about your wife?"

"Forget about her!"

"That won't do!"

"Dad, look! Chen Gang next door and Fan Pinshan across the street have all joined the volunteer army! Don't they also have wives? Pinshan's wife is even following her husband to be a medic!"

"I'm going too!" It was Lang's wife's voice.

"Good! Comrade!" Lang and his wife shook hands.

"I can't... I can't stop you, because everyone's body belongs to the country! Go! Fight and struggle for our country and nation! I won't be sad because you leave me! What makes me sad now is: our National Defense Army usually sits and eats military pay, why don't they resist when foreign enemies come? They want you, this group of immature young people, to defend against the enemy! Go! I wish you success!"

"Goodbye!" The three said in unison, leaving without looking back.

With a "bang," the door closed again.

"Alas! God! Where has our government gone?" Yuan Shu cried.

Rise Up and Take Action 237

Editor:

The conclusion of "How to Resist Japan's Research" in the clerk communication column of your newspaper on January 9 is: 1) Economic severance; 2) Preparation for armed resistance; 3) Enhancement of personal knowledge. I now have another idea: to rise up and take action. We Chinese have a big problem! We only know how to talk, but we can't act. Paper talk is not unflowery, but the reality is equal to zero. From today onwards, we should thoroughly correct our past mistakes. Those who sit and talk must be able to stand up and act.

Some people may ask, "What about yourself? Aren't you also committing this big mistake?" I dare to answer this very frankly, "No." I originally wanted to join the volunteer army. Because the government has not issued an order to send troops to recover the lost territory, where should I go to serve? I have grandparents. Although I can't bear to abandon them temporarily, I have four brothers. It doesn't matter if one person dies. So, once the government decides to issue an order to send troops to resist Japan, I can disregard everything, join the volunteer army, and kill a few enemies before dying, to fulfill my wish to "die for the country." Even before I die, if I unfortunately cannot kill the enemy (which is very common on the battlefield), then dying on the battlefield to defend the country is also seeking benevolence and attaining benevolence, and I can die in peace.

I hope that all the military officers in the country will have the same determination as General Bai, point their guns outward, and unite to resist Japan, so that I can find a place to die.

Dong Dayou Elected as the New President of the Current Session

Vice President Zhuang Jun and Accountant Lu Qianshou Reelected to Their Original Positions

Yang Xiliu Elected as Secretary

The Chinese Architects Society has been established for seven years in a blink of an eye. The number of members has increased year by year. Since the association moved into the Mainland Commercial Building on Nanjing Road last autumn, the association's affairs have become increasingly developed. At 7:30 pm on the 12th of the month, the association held its annual meeting at Zheng's private residence at No. 310 Jupless Road. That night, wax snow was flying, and the north wind was severe. Members who attended were not deterred by the cold weather and long distances. The grand occasion of that day is briefly recorded as follows.

Welcome New Members 240

The chairman of the annual meeting was the former president, Zhao Shen. After the meeting started, the chairman first introduced the new members who joined the association in the current session, and then issued certificates to the new members. The whole body applauded unanimously to show their welcome.

List of New Members 241

The association has always been strict about the qualifications for membership. The qualifications include: 1) Graduated from architectural schools at home and abroad, and have more than three years of practical experience and have a certificate; 2) Graduated from architectural schools at home and abroad, and are full-time professors of architecture and have more than three years of experience; 4) Have an industrial technician's architectural registration certificate issued by the National Government; 4) Self-employed architects for at least ten years and have solid performance certificates; 5) Handling construction matters, have achievements in improvement or invention, or have special works, or have equivalent qualifications, and have been approved by the board of directors. The new members who joined this session include Huang Yuanji, Gu Daosheng, Xu Duanfang, Miao Kaibo, Yang Runyu, Li Huibo, Wang Huabin, Ha Xiongwen, Zhang Yugang, Ding Baoxun, Zhang Kebin, Pu Hai, Ge Hongfu, Zhuang Yunchang and other fourteen people.

Reports from Various Committees 242

Reported events: 1) Chen Zhi, a member of the Preparatory Committee for the Association, reported; 2) Accountant Lu Qianshou reported on the financial situation; 3) Tong Ju, a member of the Preparatory Committee for the Association, reported; 4) Yang Xiliu, a member of the Publishing Committee, reported on the situation of the "Chinese Architecture" magazine; 5) Xu Jingzhi, a member of the Chinese Pavilion Committee for the Chicago World's Fair, reported; 6) Fan Wenzhao, a member of the Regulations and Forms Committee, reported; 7) Zhuang Jun, a member of the Architectural Terminology Committee, reported.

Matters for Discussion 243

Fan Wenzhao proposed to amend Article 8 of the association's constitution, the board of directors organization proposal. It was resolved that Article 8 of the association's constitution be amended as follows: "The board of directors of this association shall be organized by seven people. In addition to the president and vice president of the executive department as natural directors, five members who have been members for more than two years shall be elected from the regular members at the annual meeting. The chairman of the board shall be elected by the directors. Chen Zhi proposed to amend the association's membership fee proposal. It was resolved that the association's membership fee be set at 25 yuan, the annual fee be 10 yuan, and the recurring fee be 3 yuan per month. Dong Dayou proposed to temporarily cancel the association's associate member proposal. It was resolved that it be temporarily not proposed.

Results of the General Election 244

In the election of new officials for this session, the votes for the president position were initially equal among Zhao Shen, Zhuang Jun, and Dong Dayou. However, in the final vote, Dong Dayou had the most votes and was elected as the president of this session. In the election of the vice president and accountant, the results were still the reelection of the original Zhuang Jun and Lu Qianshou. Yang Xiliu was elected as the secretary of this session. The directors who were elected were Fan Wenzhao, Li Jinpei, Zhao Shen, Wu Zhenying, Luo Bangjie and other five people.

The Importance of Opening a Large Eastern Port and the Steps to Implement It (Continued) Shanghai Architectural Society 246

— Du Yange

Shanghai, holding the throat of the Yangtze River, is the convergence point of the two railways, Jinghu (Beijing-Shanghai) and Huhangyong (Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo), and a gathering place for ocean liners. Convenient transportation, finance, industry, and culture are concentrated here, creating China's only large commercial port. Furthermore, due to the instability of domestic politics and society, and the precarious lives of people in the interior, those with even a small amount of assets regard Shanghai as a haven and flock to it, causing the population to increase daily, and the outward appearance to become more prosperous. Moreover, since the National Government established its capital in Nanjing, officials and dignitaries have continuously travelled the Jinghu route, with prominent figures of the party and the nation either residing in the concessions or socializing in foreign venues. Therefore, Shanghai not only holds an important position economically, but also carries considerable political significance. The prosperity of Shanghai is indeed something that we can acknowledge with our own senses.

However, Shanghai's prosperity is inversely proportional to our national affairs. What is the reason? It can be understood by observing past events. For example, every time a man-made disaster or natural calamity occurs in the interior, Shanghai's population increases accordingly, and Shanghai's surface becomes even more prosperous. In that case, isn't such prosperity of Shanghai the same as the decline of the interior? Therefore, I say: Shanghai's prosperity is inversely proportional to national affairs. Shanghai's abnormal development is caused by the turmoil in the interior. Those with simple minds who see the superficial prosperity of Shanghai and feel complacent are no different from being deaf and blind to the overall situation. In fact, indulging in Shanghai is like a fish swimming in a pot about to boil. If we do not quickly reflect on ourselves, we will inevitably face the danger of perishing together. Writing to this point, I cannot help but shudder.

The institutions responsible for Shanghai's construction and security are three: the Municipal Government, the Public Concession's Works Department, and the French Concession's Board of Directors. The Municipal Government's jurisdiction lies in the urban areas outside the concessions, such as Nanshi (South City), Zhabei, Jiangwan, and Wusong, among which the Nanshi and Zhabei districts are relatively bustling. However, the essence of Zhabei was destroyed in the January 28th Incident, and its restoration will take time. Although Nanshi has a large population, due to historical and economic reasons, its material construction is difficult to advance rapidly. Commercial activities are also unable to compete with the concessions due to the psychology and habits of the people. As for the city center, due to the Municipal Government's financial difficulties after the January 28th Incident and the general trend of people moving towards the western districts, it could not maintain its initial rapid development.

The situation of Shanghai's areas under the Municipal Government's jurisdiction is as described above. It can be seen that the so-called prosperous Shanghai is only the Public Concession and the French Concession, manipulated by foreigners. Therefore, to praise Shanghai as the second New York or the second London is merely to praise foreigners' Shanghai. How can one not feel ashamed speaking of this?

However, the wealth to build a prosperous Shanghai is the lifeblood of us, the yellow-skinned, black-eyed owners of this land. To have our own wealth taken by foreigners to build their prosperous Shanghai shows a glimpse of our compatriots' indolence. To live peacefully in the concessions without any sense of alarm shows that we only have the servility to rely on others and lack the spirit of independence and creation.

Now, everyone should be able to awaken, right? We must rely on our own spirit, intelligence, and wealth to open up our own commercial port to wash away past shame and reclaim our rights and interests. The large port of the Orient, close to Shanghai, is the commercial port designated by Sun Yat-sen. It is superior to Shanghai in terms of geography and human resources. Once successfully opened, its future prosperity will not be difficult to surpass Shanghai. However, we must make efforts as soon as possible to prevent foreigners from getting there first, because there are many foreigners coveting this unique and superior commercial port in the East.

Compatriots with wealth and intelligence, quickly rise up and plan for it! And hope that the government authorities will encourage and assist it with the power of the nation, so that it can be realized in the shortest possible time! Because this is a major construction project related to the economic prosperity and decline of the entire country! (To be continued)

The Content of the Ufa Film Studio 251

— Xin Fu

A tourist who came out of the "New Babylon City" Neubabelsberg Ufa film studio said to others: "Now I know why this place is called "New Babylon City". It turns out that when they work, they speak languages from all over the world, just like when they built the Tower of Babel in the past."

The Ufa film studio occupies an area of over ninety acres. There, there are forty-two large buildings: and many open spaces, building many streets, palaces, thatched cottages, mansions, pastures, forests, pools, bridges and various things used when making films. In those large buildings, there are fourteen one-story and two-story buildings that are warehouses for raw materials and properties, six power plants, three cellars for storing copies, and a large cellar dedicated to storing original film. In addition, there are two very large office buildings, with an average of six to seven hundred workers.

There are a total of three hundred and fifty telephone lines in the film studio, all using automatic machines. Furthermore, the police rules are of course very strict and orderly. "No smoking" signs are everywhere. There are a total of nineteen firefighters stationed in the studio, divided into three locations.

There are two very large and two smaller buildings with nine sound stages. The most magnificent building is the tall building built in 1926 by the famous engineer Staurak, which occupies an area of nine thousand square yards. Inside, there are three large theaters. Around the theaters, there are fifty partitions used as dressing rooms, bathrooms, and makeup rooms for the actors, and the offices of the directors are also included.

There is also another film studio, built in 1929, occupying an area of three thousand eight hundred square yards, with four sound stages inside. The walls and roof are built according to acoustic principles, so there is no interference from noise. Even the sound of thunder during heavy wind and rain cannot penetrate inside. This kind of architecture is indeed worthy of praise. As for everything else about Ufa, I will talk about it another day!

Tom Mix's Horse 252

— Han

The horsemanship of the horse star Tom Mix can be said to be the most famous in Hollywood. His horse is named Tony, and it can also be regarded as a famous horse that has "experienced many battles". They, one man and one horse, have earned a salary of 7.5 million yuan in the twenty years from 1912 to the present. But when Tom bought that horse in Arizona, he only paid twelve dollars and fifty cents, which is absolutely true.

Now Tony is getting old and retiring due to his increasing age. He enjoys his twilight years in the forest, which is quite entertaining. During his peak, he also traveled to Europe, lived in the stables of the Prince of England, attended a grand banquet held by Londoners at the Savoy Hotel for him and his master, and was ridden by Tom to take an elevator to the top of the Eiffel Tower, the world's largest building.

Laughton's Nest 255

— Zhongqin

When Charles Laughton was in England, he and his wife built a thatched cottage in a secluded place a few miles away from Surrey, where the ancient trees are towering, in the space with the densest shade. He and his wife lived in this thatched cottage. But in the summer, they moved again, building the grass house on top of the trees. The top is still covered with more lush leaves, and they use a long ladder to get in and out. When his friends came to visit him, none of them did not frown and ask him why he did this. He said that it was because he admired the characters of ancient times, so he practiced the life of ancient times. Many people thought he was poor, but his property was actually not small, so this reason is not sufficient. This can only be regarded as one of his quirks.

When he arrived in the United States, he built a thatched cottage in Hollywood in the same way, living on the ground in winter and living on top of the trees in summer. This joke spread throughout the United States, because the whole United States only has thirty-story, sixty-story, one-hundred-story, and even one-hundred-and-fifty-story skyscrapers, but there has never been a retro-style house built on top of trees, so they spread it as a joke.

Wardrobe Room in American Film Studios 256

— Zongwen

American film studios pay great attention to the wardrobe department. Because in recent years, they often make wordless plays that were popular in the past into films. The stories they tell mostly contain three eras: the first era is around 1860, the second era is around 1885, and the third era is the present day. To prepare the costumes for these three eras, one must pay special attention to it, and carefully study which era is which kind of costume with an artistic eye, without the slightest confusion. Therefore, some film studios have several wardrobe rooms with different eras, often storing thousands of different clothes. However, the women who manage the costumes must have graduated from art school, and also have experience on stage and in film performances. If clothing from 1860 is needed at a certain time, she will immediately have that type of clothing. In addition to the women who manage the clothes in the clothing department, there are also many seamstresses who specialize in making various modern clothes, as well as imitating many clothes that were popular in ancient times.

Soviet Sound Films Coming to Shanghai 257

— Shi

Shanghai people will soon have the opportunity to watch precious Soviet film art. This film was produced by the Soviet film trust "Intorgkino". Introductions to the two films "Two Meetings" and "Road to Life" have already been published in the newspapers. The basic value of Soviet films lies in the selection of themes. Soviet films mostly draw materials from the actual daily lives of the masses and their adherence to objective facts. Ulinov's "Two Meetings" is a representative work of Soviet sound films, with both material and technology reaching a superior level. The musical classics composed by Blok added a lot of artistic strength to the film. Like "Road to Life", this film is warmly welcomed everywhere it is screened. "Road to Life" was the first Soviet sound film to be screened in China. When the film opened in Harbin last January, the total number of viewers exceeded 32,000 in one week. This film became the most popular film in Harbin.
